CockroachDB v24.3 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a> is a required <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases#major-versions" data-versioned="true">Regular release</a>.

Refer to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">Major release types</a> before installing or upgrading for release timing and support details. To learn what's new in this release, refer to its [Feature Highlights](#feature-highlights).

On this page, you can read about changes and find downloads for all production and testing releases of CockroachDB v24.3 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-phases" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a>

- For key feature enhancements in v24.3 and other upgrade considerations, refer to the notes for [v24.3.0](#v24-3-0).
- For details about release types, naming, and licensing, refer to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases" data-versioned="true">Releases</a> page.
- Be sure to also review the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy" data-versioned="true">Release Support Policy</a>.
- After downloading a supported CockroachDB binary, learn how to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/install-cockroachdb" data-versioned="true">install CockroachDB</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrade your cluster</a>.

Get future release notes emailed to you:

<MarketoEmailForm />

## v24.3.29

Release Date: March 9, 2026

### Downloads

<Note>
This version is currently available only for select CockroachDB Cloud clusters. To request to upgrade a CockroachDB self-hosted cluster to this version, [contact support](https://support.cockroachlabs.com/hc/requests/new).
</Note>

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.28...v24.3.29](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.28...v24.3.29)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where AVRO file imports of data with JSON or binary records could hang indefinitely when encountering stream errors from cloud storage (such as `HTTP/2` `CANCEL` errors). Import jobs will now properly fail with an error instead of hanging. [#161438](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/161438)
- Fixed a bug that, in rare cases, could cause a node to crash when using a changefeed with the `end_time` option. [#161678](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/161678)
- Fixed a bug that could cause changefeeds using Kafka v1 sinks to hang when the changefeed was cancelled. [#162117](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/162117)
- Fixed a bug where generating a debug zip could trigger an out-of-memory (OOM) condition on a node if malformed log entries were present in logs using `json` or `json-compact` formatting. This bug was introduced in v24.1. [#163360](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/163360)

### Miscellaneous

- Fixed a bug where import rollback could incorrectly revert data in a table that was already online. This could only occur if an import job was cancelled or failed after the import had already succeeded and the table was made available for use. [#159900](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/159900)

Release Date: March 5, 2026

Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.28
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.28 on Github, visit [v24.3.28 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.28).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.27...v24.3.28](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.27...v24.3.28)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where an internal context structure could grow unboundedly over time. In rare cases, on nodes running continuously for several months or more, this could cause the `cockroach` process to appear stalled when a CPU profile was requested.​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​​ [#164778](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/164778)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.27
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.27 on Github, visit [v24.3.27 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.27).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.26...v24.3.27](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.26...v24.3.27)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a rare race condition between range splits and MVCC garbage collection where a GCRequest could target keys outside its declared span. In rare cases, this could result in data on the post-split right-hand side (RHS) being incorrectly garbage collected, potentially leading to lost writes. The system now detects and rejects such malformed GC requests. [#163774](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/163774)
- Fixed a bug where generating a debug zip could trigger an out-of-memory (OOM) condition on a node if malformed log entries were present in logs using json or json-compact formatting. Debug zip generation now safely handles malformed log lines and prevents excessive memory consumption. [#163800](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/163800)

### Docker image

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.26 on Github, visit [v24.3.26 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.26).

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where `IMPORT` with Avro data using `OCF` format could silently lose data if the underlying storage (e.g., S3) returned an error during read. Such errors are now properly reported. Other formats (specified via `data_as_binary_records` and `data_as_json_records` options) are unaffected. The bug has been present since approximately v20.1. [#161321](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/161321)

## v24.3.25

Release Date: January 9, 2026

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.25
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.25 on Github, visit [v24.3.25 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.25).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.24...v24.3.25](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.24...v24.3.25)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause incorrect query results when using prepared statements with *NULL* placeholders. The bug has existed since v21.2 and violated SQL *NULL* -equality semantics by returning rows with *NULL* values when the result set should have been empty. From v21.2 to v25.3, the bug occurred when all of the following were true:
    - The query was run with an explicit or implicit prepared statement
    - The query had an equality filter on a placeholder and a `UNIQUE` column
    - The column contained *NULL* values
    - The placeholder was assigned to *NULL* during execution
    - Starting in v25.4, the requirements to trigger the bug were loosened: the column no longer needed to be `UNIQUE`, and the bug could be reproduced if the column was included in any index. [#159078](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/159078)
- Fixed a race condition that could occur during context cancellation of an incoming snapshot. [#159538](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/159538)
- Fixed a bug causing a query predicate to be ignored when the predicate was on a column following one or more `ENUM` columns in an index, the predicate constrained the column to multiple values, and a lookup join to the index was chosen for the query plan. This bug was introduced in 24.3.0 and has been present in all versions since. [#159774](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/159774)

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.23 on Github, visit [v24.3.23 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.23).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.22...v24.3.23](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.22...v24.3.23)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `sql.statements.bytes_read.count` metric that counts the number of bytes scanned by SQL statements. [#156598](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156598)
- Added the `sql.statements.index_rows_written.count` metric that counts the number of primary and secondary index rows modified by SQL statements. [#156598](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156598)
- Added the `sql.statements.index_bytes_written.count` metric that counts the number of primary and secondary index bytes modified by SQL statements. [#156598](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156598)
- Added the `sql.statements.rows_read.count` metric that counts the number of index rows read by SQL statements. [#156598](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156598)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the job responsible for compacting stats for the SQL activity state could enter an unschedulable state. [#155971](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/155971)
- Fixed a bug where changefeeds using CDC queries could sometimes unexpectedly fail after a schema change with a descriptor retrieval error. [#156549](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156549)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in the `cockroach node drain` command where draining a node using virtual clusters (such as clusters running Physical Cluster Replication (PCR)) could return before the drain was complete, possibly resulting in shutting down the node while it still had active SQL clients and range leases. [#156311](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/156311)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.21
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.21 on Github, visit [v24.3.21 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.21).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.20...v24.3.21](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.20...v24.3.21)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where an `INSERT` statement could fail with a type checking error while adding a `BIT(n)` column. [#153604](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/153604)
- Fixed a bug that caused panics when executing `COPY` into a table with hidden columns and expression indexes. The panic only occurred when the session setting `expect_and_ignore_not_visible_columns_in_copy` was enabled. This bug was introduced with `expect_and_ignore_not_visible_columns_in_copy` in v22.1.0. [#154284](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/154284)
- Fixed a bug where the presence of duplicate temporary tables in a backup caused the restore to fail with an error containing the text `restoring table desc and namespace entries: table already exists`. [#154399](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/154399)

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.20
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.20 on Github, visit [v24.3.20 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.20).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.19...v24.3.20](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.19...v24.3.20)

### SQL language changes

- When `sql_safe_updates` is enabled, the `ALTER TABLE... LOCALITY` statement will be blocked when trying to convert an existing table to `REGIONAL BY ROW`, unless a region column has been added to the table. This protects against undesired behavior that caused `UPDATE` or `DELETE` statements to fail against the table while the locality change was in progress. [#152602](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152602)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where invalid default expressions could cause backfilling schema changes to retry forever. [#147015](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147015)
- Fixed a bug that could cause excessive memory allocations when compacting timeseries keys. [#151813](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151813)
- Fixed a bug where updating column default expressions would incorrectly remove sequence ownerships for the affected column. [#152313](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152313)
- Fixed a bug that allowed foreign-key violations to result from some combinations of concurrent `READ COMMITTED` and `SERIALIZABLE` transactions. If both `SERIALIZABLE` and weaker-isolation transactions will concurrently modify rows involved in foreign-key relationships, the `SERIALIZABLE` transactions must have the following session variables set in order to prevent any possible foreign-key violations:
    - `SET enable_implicit_fk_locking_for_serializable = on;`
    - `SET enable_shared_locking_for_serializable = on;`
    - `SET enable_durable_locking_for_serializable = on;` [#152376](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152376)
- Added an automatic repair for dangling or invalid entries in the `system.comments` table. [#152468](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152468)
- Fixed a bug where views could not reference the `crdb_region` column from their underlying tables in expressions. [#152742](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152742)

### Performance improvements

- Lookup joins can now be used on tables with virtual columns even if the type of the search argument is not identical to the column type referenced in the virtual column. [#152630](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152630)

### Miscellaneous

- Tunes S3 client retry behavior to be more reliable in the presence of correlated errors. [#151875](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151875)

### Docker image


### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.19 on Github, visit [v24.3.19 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.19).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.18...v24.3.19](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.18...v24.3.19)

### General changes

- Backporting detailed error logging logic gated behind a cluster setting. The cluster setting enables detailed error logging for messages exceeding Kafka v2 size limit. [#150182](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/150182)
- Changefeeds emitting to Kafka sinks that were created in CockroachDB v24.2.1+, or v23.2.10+ and v24.1.4+ with the `changefeed.new_kafka_sink.enabled` cluster setting enabled now include the message key, size, and MVCC timestamp in "message too large" error logs. [#150182](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/150182)

### Operational changes

- Introduced a cluster setting, `sql.stats.error_on_concurrent_create_stats.enabled`, which modifies how CockroachDB reacts to concurrent auto stats jobs. The default, `true`, maintains the previous behavior. Setting `sql.stats.error_on_concurrent_create_stats.enabled` to `false` will cause the concurrent auto stats job to be skipped with just a log entry and no increased error counters. [#149841](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/149841)
- Updated TTL job replanning to be less sensitive by focusing specifically on detecting when nodes become unavailable rather than reacting to all plan differences. The cluster setting `sql.ttl.replan_flow_threshold` may have been set to `0` to work around the TTL replanner being too sensitive; this fix will alleviate that and any instance that had set `replan_flow_threshold` to `0` can be reset back to the default. [#151489](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151489)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed an issue where the `mvcc_timestamp` field was incorrectly returning zero values when used with CDC queries. The timestamp is now emitted correctly. [#147112](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147112)
- Fixed a bug that would allow a race condition in foreign key cascades under `READ COMMITTED` and `REPEATABLE READ` isolation levels. [#150336](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/150336)
- Fixed a bug that could cause some errors returned by attempts to upload backup data to external storage providers to be undetected, potentially causing incomplete backups. [#151081](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151081)
- Fixed a memory accounting issue in the client certificate cache that caused multiple allocations to be reported for the same certificate. The cache now accurately tracks memory usage and includes a safeguard to prevent it from negatively affecting SQL operations. [#151141](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151141)
- Fixed a bug where `debug.zip` files collected from clusters with `disallow_full_table_scans` enabled were missing system table data. [#151223](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151223)

### Build changes

- Upgrade Go to consume security fixes [#150989](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/150989)

### Miscellaneous

- Restore will now re-attempt `AdminSplit` KV requests instead of immediately failing and pausing the job. [#149619](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/149619)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.17
```

- Fixed a bug that could cause some errors returned by attempts to upload backup data to external storage providers to be undetected, potentially causing incomplete backups. [#151094](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/151094)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.16
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.16 on Github, visit [v24.3.16 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.16).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.15...v24.3.16](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.15...v24.3.16)

### SQL language changes

- Added a session variable `initial_retry_backoff_for_read_committed` that controls the initial backoff duration when retrying an individual statement in an explicit `READ COMMITTED` transaction. A duration of `0` disables exponential backoff. If a statement in an explicit `READ COMMITTED` transaction is failing with the `40001` error `ERROR: restart transaction: read committed retry limit exceeded; set by max_retries_for_read_committed=...`, then you should set `initial_retry_backoff_for_read_committed` to a duration proportional to the typical execution time of the statement (in addition to also increasing `max_retries_for_read_committed` ). [#148228](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148228)
- Added the metrics `sql.txn.auto_retry.count` and `sql.statements.auto_retry.count`, which count the number of automatic retries of SQL transactions and statements, respectively, within the database. These metrics differ from the related `txn.restarts.*` metrics, which count retryable errors emitted by the KV layer that must be retried. The new `sql.txn.auto_retry.count` and `sql.statements.auto_retry.count` metrics count auto-retry actions taken by the SQL layer in response to some of those retryable errors. [#148228](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148228)

### Operational changes

- Introduced a cluster setting, `sql.stats.error_on_concurrent_create_stats.enabled`, which modifies how CockroachDB reacts to concurrent auto stats jobs. The default, `true`, maintains the previous behavior. Setting `sql.stats.error_on_concurrent_create_stats.enabled` to `false` will cause the concurrent auto stats job to be skipped with just a log entry and no increased error counters. [#149850](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/149850)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a data race in the `cloudstorage` sink. [#147161](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147161)
- Fixed an error in `crdb_internal.table_spans` that could occur when a table's schema had been dropped. [#148048](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148048)
- Fixed a bug where `libpq` clients using the async API could hang with large result sets (Python: psycopg; Ruby: ActiveRecord, ruby-pg). [#148470](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148470)
- The `RESET ALL` statement no longer affects the following session variables:
    - `is_superuser`
    - `role`
    - `session_authorization`
    - `transaction_isolation`
    - `transaction_priority`
    - `transaction_status`
    - `transaction_read_only`

        This better matches PostgreSQL behavior for `RESET ALL`. In addition, the `DISCARD ALL` statement no longer errors when `default_transaction_use_follower_reads` is enabled. [#149431](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/149431)
- Fixed a bug that would allow a race condition in foreign key cascades under `READ COMMITTED` and `REPEATABLE READ` isolation levels. [#150342](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/150342)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.15
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.15 on Github, visit [v24.3.15 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.15).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.14...v24.3.15](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.14...v24.3.15)

### SQL language changes

- Added the metrics `sql.txn.auto_retry.count` and `sql.statements.auto_retry.count`, which count the number of automatic retries of SQL transactions and statements, respectively, within the database. These metrics differ from the related `txn.restarts.*` metrics, which count retryable errors emitted by the KV layer that must be retried. The new `sql.txn.auto_retry.count` and `sql.statements.auto_retry.count` metrics count auto-retry actions taken by the SQL layer in response to some of those retryable errors. [#148229](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148229)
- Added a session variable `initial_retry_backoff_for_read_committed` that controls the initial backoff duration when retrying an individual statement in an explicit `READ COMMITTED` transaction. A duration of `0` disables exponential backoff. If a statement in an explicit `READ COMMITTED` transaction is failing with the `40001` error `ERROR: restart transaction: read committed retry limit exceeded; set by max_retries_for_read_committed=...`, then you should set `initial_retry_backoff_for_read_committed` to a duration proportional to the typical execution time of the statement (in addition to also increasing `max_retries_for_read_committed` ). [#148229](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/148229)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause an `AFTER` trigger to fail with `client already committed or rolled back the transaction` if the query also contained foreign-key cascades. The bug had existed since `AFTER` triggers were introduced in v24.3. [#146974](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146974)
- Fixed a bug that could potentially cause a changefeed to complete erroneously when one of its watched tables encounters a schema change. [#147031](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147031)
- Fixed a bug that caused the SQL Activity &gt; Statement Fingerprint page to fail to load details for statements run with application names containing a `#` character. [#147221](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147221)
- Fixed a bug that could cause the `cockroach` process to `segfault` when collecting runtime execution traces (typically collected via the **Advanced Debug** page in the Console). [#147337](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147337)
- Fixed a bug that caused the optimizer to ignore index hints when optimizing some forms of prepared statements. This could result in one of two unexpected behaviors: a query errors with the message `index cannot be used for this query` when the index can actually be used; or a query uses an index that does not adhere to the hint. The hints relevant to this bug are regular index hints, e.g., `SELECT * FROM tab@index`, `FORCE_INVERTED_INDEX`, and `FORCE_ZIGZAG`. [#147415](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147415)
- Fixed the database filter in the DB Console's Hot Ranges page, which was broken in v24.3.3, and updated the locality filter to remove duplicate entries. [#147444](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147444)
- Fixed a bug that could cause stable expressions to be folded in cached query plans. The bug could cause stable expressions like `current_setting` to return the wrong result if used in a prepared statement. The bug was introduced in v23.2.22, v24.1.14, v24.3.9, v25.1.2, and the v25.2 alpha. [#147458](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147458)
- Fixed a bug where prepared statements on schema changes could fail with runtime errors. [#147669](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147669)
- Fixed a bug where `ALTER TABLE` was modifying identity attributes on columns not backed by a sequence. [#147768](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147768)
- Fixed an issue with logical data replication (LDR) where the presence of a unique index could have caused spurious dead-letter queue (DLQ) entries if the unique index had a smaller index ID than the primary key index. [#147354](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147354)

### Performance improvements

- TTL jobs now respond to cluster topology changes by restarting and rebalancing across available nodes. [#147211](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147211)

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.14 on Github, visit [v24.3.14 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.14).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.13...v24.3.14](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.13...v24.3.14)

### Operational changes

- Changed the default value of the cluster setting `admission.l0_file_count_overload_threshold` to `4000`. [#145919](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145919)
- SQL queries run on the source cluster by logical data replication (LDR) and physical cluster replication (PCR) will account to internal metrics like `sql.statements.active.internal` instead of the metrics like `sql.statements.active` that are used to monitor application workload. [#145114](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145114)

### DB Console changes

- Schema insights that recommend replacing an index were previously a two-statement command consisting of a `CREATE INDEX` and a `DROP INDEX` statement. When these two DDL statements were run as a single batched command, it was possible for one statement to succeed and one to fail. This is because DDL statements do not have the same atomicity guarantees as other SQL statements in CockroachDB. Index-replacement insights are now a single `CREATE INDEX` statement followed by a comment with additional DDL statements to be run manually: an `ALTER INDEX... NOT VISIBLE` statement, which makes the old index invisible to the optimizer, followed by a `DROP INDEX` statement that should only be run after making the old index invisible and verifying that workload performance is satisfactory. [#145988](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145988)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where using values `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter` and `min_checkpoint_frequency` such that `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter * min_checkpoint_frequency < 1` would cause a panic. Jitter will now be disabled in this case. [#144425](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144425)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console where the **Drop unused index** tag appeared multiple times for an index on the **Indexes** tab of the table details page. [#144652](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144652)
- Fixed the following bugs in the **Schedules** page of the DB Console:
    - Fixed a bug where the **Schedules** page displayed only a subset of a cluster's schedules. The **Schedules** page now correctly displays all schedules.
    - Fixed a bug where manually updating the `show` or `status` parameters in the URL (e.g., `http://127.0.0.1:8080/#/schedules?status=ACTIVE&show=50` ) caused the **Schedules** page to fail to load. [#144805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144805)
- Fixed a bug in the **SQL Activity Statements** page where filtering by **Statement Type** returned no results. The filter now works as expected. [#144854](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144854)
- Improved the performance of `SHOW CREATE TABLE` on multi-region databases with large numbers of objects. [#145073](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145073)
- Fixed a bug where running `DROP INDEX` on a hash-sharded index did not properly detect dependencies from functions and procedures on the shard column. This caused the `DROP INDEX` statement to fail with an internal validation error. Now the statement returns a correct error message, and using `DROP INDEX... CASCADE` works as expected by dropping the dependent functions and procedures. [#145392](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145392)
- Fixed a bug where a node that was drained as part of decommissioning may have interrupted SQL connections that were still active during drain (and for which drain would have been expected to wait). [#145447](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145447)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to schema changes hanging after a cluster recovered from availability issues. [#145543](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145543)
- Previously, on a table with multiple column families, CockroachDB could encounter a `Non-nullable column "‹×›:‹×›" with no value` error in rare cases during table statistics collection. The bug was present since v19.2 and is now fixed. [#145574](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145574)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a row-level TTL job to fail with the error "comparison of two different versions of enum" if an `ENUM` type referenced by the table experienced a schema change. [#145915](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145915)
- Fixed a bug where the physical cluster replication (PCR) reader catalog job could hit validation errors when schema objects had dependencies between them (for example, when a sequence's default expression was being removed). [#145997](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145997)
- Fixed a bug where orphaned leases were not properly cleaned up. [#146096](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146096)
- Fixed an internal assertion failure that could occur during operations like `ALTER TYPE` or `ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION` when temporary tables were present. [#146198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146198)
- Fixed a bug that could cause queries that perform work in parallel to ignore the requested quality-of-service level. Affected operations include lookup joins, DistSQL execution, and foreign-key checks. [#146222](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146222)
- Fixed a bug that prevented `TRUNCATE` from succeeding if any indexes on the table had back-reference dependencies, such as from a view or function referencing the index. [#146324](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146324)
- Fixed a bug where an invalid comment in the `system.comment` table for a schema object could make it inaccessible. [#146416](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146416)
- Fixed a bug in the rangefeed restarts metric that was introduced in v23.2. [#133978](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133978)
- Fixed a rare corruption bug that impacts import and materialized views. [#144661](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144661)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.13
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.13 on Github, visit [v24.3.13 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.13).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.12...v24.3.13](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.12...v24.3.13)

### Operational changes

- The default value of the `admission.l0_file_count_overload_threshold` cluster setting is now `4000`. This change improves stability under high write load and during Write-Ahead Log (WAL) failover by addressing token exhaustion. [#146597](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146597)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.12
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.12 on Github, visit [v24.3.12 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.12).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.11...v24.3.12](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.11...v24.3.12)

### General changes

- CockroachDB v24.3.12 and subsequent v24.3 releases are eligible for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">long term support (LTS)</a>.

### SQL language changes

- Added the `WITH IGNORE_FOREIGN_KEYS` option to `SHOW CREATE TABLE` which omits foreign key constraints from the output schema. This option is also allowed in `SHOW CREATE VIEW`, but has no effect. It cannot be combined with the `WITH REDACT` option. [#142162](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142162)
- `EXPLAIN ANALYZE` statements now display the number of transaction retries and time spent retrying, if non-zero, in the plan output. [#142929](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142929)
- A new `execution time` statistic is now reported on `EXPLAIN ANALYZE` output for most operators. Previously, this statistic was only available on the DistSQL diagrams in `EXPLAIN ANALYZE (DISTSQL)` output. [#143897](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143897)

### Operational changes

- Added the cluster setting `server.child_metrics.include_aggregate.enabled` (default: `true` ) that controls the behavior of Prometheus child metrics reporting ( `/_status/vars` ). When set to `true`, child metrics include an aggregate time series, maintaining the existing behavior. When set to `false`, it stops reporting the aggregate time series, preventing double counting when querying metrics. [#142745](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142745)
- The `sys.cpu.host.combined.percent-normalized` metric has been updated to include additional counters for more accurate host CPU measurement and to reduce underreporting. It now accounts for time spent processing hardware ( `irq` ) and software ( `softirq` ) interrupts, as well as `nice` time, which represents low-priority user-mode activity. [#142905](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142905)
- The `server.client_cert_expiration_cache.capacity` cluster setting has been removed. The `security.certificate.expiration.client` and `security.certificate.ttl.client` metrics now report the lowest value observed for a user in the last 24 hours. [#143591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143591)
- SQL queries run on the source cluster by logical data replication (LDR) and physical cluster replication (PCR) will account to internal metrics like `sql.statements.active.internal` instead of the metrics like `sql.statements.active` that are used to monitor application workload. [#145115](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145115)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in client certificate expiration metrics, `security.certificate.expiration.client` and `security.certificate.ttl.client`. [#142843](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142843)
- Fast failback could succeed even if the standby cluster protected timestamp had been removed, causing the reverse physical cluster replication (PCR) stream to enter a crashing loop. This patch ensures the failback command fast fails. [#143078](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143078)
- Fixed a bug that caused changefeeds to fail on startup when scanning a single key. [#143149](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143149)
- MVCC garbage collection is now fully subject to IO admission control. Previously, it was possible for MVCC GC to cause store overload (such as LSM inversion) when a large amount of data would become eligible for garbage collection. Should any issues arise from subjecting MVCC GC to admission control, the `kv.mvcc_gc.queue_kv_admission_control.enabled` cluster setting can be set to `false` to restore the previous behavior. [#143276](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143276)
- Fixed a bug where calling a stored procedure could drop the procedure if it had `OUT` parameters that were not used by the calling routine. This bug had existed since PL/pgSQL `CALL` statements were introduced in v24.1. [#143289](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143289)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would encounter an internal error when decoding the gists of plans with `CALL` statements. The bug had been present since v23.2. [#143314](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143314)
- The reader virtual cluster now starts if the user begins a physical cluster replication (PCR) stream from a cursor via `ALTER VIRTUAL CLUSTER virtual_cluster START REPLICATION OF virtual_cluster ON pgurl_physical_cluster WITH READ VIRTUAL CLUSTER`. [#143369](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143369)
- Fixed a crash due to "use of enum metadata before hydration" when using logical data replication (LDR) with user-defined types (UDTs). [#143376](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143376)
- Fixed a potential deadlock that could occur during client certificate updates while metrics were being collected. This issue affected the reliability of certificate expiration reporting. [#143591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143591)
- Fixed a bug in v24.1.14, v24.3.7, v24.3.8, and v25.1 that could cause a nil-pointer error when a column's default expression contained a volatile expression (like `nextval` ) as a UDF argument. [#143636](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143636)
- Previously, the fields `maximum memory usage` and `max sql temp disk usage` in the `EXPLAIN ANALYZE` output could be under-reported for distributed plans when memory-intensive operations were fully performed on the remote nodes. This is now fixed. The bug existed in v22.1 and later. [#143793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143793)
- The `ALTER VIRTUAL CLUSTER SET REPLICATION READ VIRTUAL CLUSTER` syntax is now supported for adding a reader virtual cluster for an existing PCR standby. [#143905](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143905)
- Previously, whenever CockroachDB collected a statement bundle when plan-gist-based matching was used, `plan.txt` would be incomplete. This is now fixed. The bug had been present since the introduction of plan-gist-based matching in v23.1, and was partially addressed in v24.2. [#143935](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143935)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could encounter a `cannot specify timestamp older than...` error during table statistics collection in some cases (e.g., when the cluster is overloaded). The bug was present since v19.1. [#144017](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144017)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a stack overflow during execution of a prepared statement that invoked a PL/pgSQL routine with a loop. The bug existed in versions v23.2.22, v24.1.15, v24.3.9, v25.1.2, v25.1.3, and pre-release versions of v25.2 prior to v25.2.0-alpha.3. [#144030](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144030)
- Fixed a rare corruption bug that impacts `IMPORT` and materialized views. [#144688](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144688)

## v24.3.11

Release Date: April 28, 2025

### Downloads

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.11.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>Windows<br/>(Experimental)</td><td>Intel</td><td><a ### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.11
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.11 on Github, visit [v24.3.11 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.11).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.10...v24.3.11](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.10...v24.3.11)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a rare corruption bug that impacts import and materialized views. [#144661](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144661)

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.9...v24.3.10](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.9...v24.3.10)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause a stack overflow during execution of a prepared statement that invoked a PL/pgSQL routine with a loop. The bug existed in versions v23.2.22, v24.1.15, v24.3.9, v25.1.2, v25.1.3, and pre-release versions of v25.2 prior to v25.2.0-alpha.3. [#144060](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144060)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.9
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.9 on Github, visit [v24.3.9 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.9).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.8...v24.3.9](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.8...v24.3.9)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `WITH IGNORE_FOREIGN_KEYS` option to `SHOW CREATE TABLE`, which omits foreign key constraints from the output schema. This option is also allowed in `SHOW CREATE VIEW`, but has no effect. It cannot be combined with the `WITH REDACT` option. [#143368](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143368)

### Operational changes

- Added the `sql.transaction_timeout.count` metric to track the number of SQL statements that fail due to exceeding the transaction timeout. [#142156](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142156)
- Added the `sql.statement_timeout.count` to track the number of SQL statements that fail due to exceeding the statement timeout. [#142156](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142156)
- The `server.client_cert_expiration_cache.capacity` cluster setting has been removed. The `security.certificate.expiration.client` and `security.certificate.ttl.client` metrics now report the lowest value observed for a user in the last 24 hours. [#143593](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143593)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that prevented starting multi-table Logical Data Replication (LDR) streams on tables that used user-defined types. [#141793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141793)
- The TTL deletion job now includes a retry mechanism that progressively reduces the batch size when encountering contention. This improves the chances of successful deletion without requiring manual adjustments to TTL knobs. Also added the `jobs.row_level_ttl.num_delete_batch_retries` metric to track the number of times the TTL job had to reduce the batch size and try again. [#142323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142323)
- Fixed a bug when running with the `autocommit_before_ddl` session setting that could cause a runtime error when binding a previously prepared DDL statement. [#141987](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141987)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate casts to some OID types (like `REGCLASS` ) in some cases. The bug had been present since at least v22.1. [#141958](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141958)
- Fixed a bug that could cause gateway nodes to panic when performing an `UPSERT` on a table with a `BOOL` primary key column and a partial index with the primary key column as the predicate expression. [#141823](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141823)
- Fixed a bug that would prevent the `CREATE TRIGGER` and `DROP TRIGGER` statements from working if the `autocommit_before_ddl` setting was enabled, and if the statement was either sent as a prepared statement or as part of a batch of multiple statements. [#142303](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142303)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `SHOW TABLES` and other introspection operations to encounter a `batch timestamp must be after replica GC threshold` error. [#141720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141720)
- Fixed a bug where Physical Cluster Replication (PCR) reader catalogs could have orphaned rows in `system.namespace` after an object is renamed. [#142873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142873)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `nil pointer dereference` errors when executing statements with user-defined functions (UDFs). The error could also occur when executing statements with some built-in functions, like `obj_description`. [#141652](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141652)
- Fixed a bug in `v24.1.14`, `v24.3.7`, `v24.3.8`, and `v25.1` that could cause a nil-pointer error when a column's default expression contained a volatile expression (like `nextval` ) as a UDF argument. [#143635](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143635)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent `SHOW CREATE TABLE` from working if a database was offline (e.g., due to a `RESTORE` on that database). [#141509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141509)
- Fixed an issue where dropping a database with triggers could fail due to an undropped backreference to a trigger function. [#142726](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142726)
- Fixed a bug where the declarative schema changer allowed `CREATE SEQUENCE` operations to proceed even while a `DROP SCHEMA` or `DROP DATABASE` was in progress. Such operations now retry if the parent object has a schema change in progress, preventing new child objects from being created under deleted parent objects. [#142763](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142763)
- Fixed a potential deadlock that could occur during client certificate updates while metrics were being collected. This issue affected the reliability of certificate expiration reporting. [#143593](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143593)
- Fixed a bug where the fraction completed and internal checkpoints during an index backfill operation would stop getting written if any of the periodic fraction/checkpoint write operations failed. Progress is now logged in addition to being written to the job record. This bug affected schema change operations such as creating an index or adding a non-nullable column to a table. [#141787](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141787)
- Fixed a crash due to `use of enum metadata before hydration` when using logical data replication (LDR) with user-defined types. [#143389](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143389)

### Miscellaneous

- When configuring the `sql.ttl.default_delete_rate_limit` cluster setting, a notice is now displayed informing the user that the TTL rate limit is per leaseholder per table with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">link to the docs</a>. [#142833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142833)
- Improved S3 credential caching for AWS Security Token Service (STS) credentials. [#142437](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142437)

### Bug fixes

- Improved S3 credential caching for STS credentials to avoid exceeding the Amazon metadata service rate limit and encountering errors related to AssumeRole API calls when accessing large numbers of files in larger clusters. [#142679](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142679)

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.7.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.7.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v24.3.7.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.7.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>ARM</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.7.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v24.3.7.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a ### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.7
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.7 on Github, visit [v24.3.7 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.7).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.6...v24.3.7](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.6...v24.3.7)

### SQL language changes

- Added support for a new index hint, `AVOID_FULL_SCAN`, which will prevent the optimizer from planning a full scan for the specified table if any other plan is possible. The hint can be used in the same way as other existing index hints. For example, `SELECT * FROM table_name@{AVOID_FULL_SCAN};`. This hint is similar to `NO_FULL_SCAN`, but will not error if a full scan cannot be avoided. Note that a full scan of a partial index would not normally be considered a "full scan" for the purposes of the `AVOID_FULL_SCAN` and `NO_FULL_SCAN` hints, but if the user has explicitly forced the partial index via `FORCE_INDEX=index_name`, it is considered a full scan. [#140255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140255) [#140998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140998)
- Added the `optimizer_prefer_bounded_cardinality` session setting, which instructs the optimizer to prefer query plans where every expression has a guaranteed upper-bound on the number of rows it will process. This may help the optimizer produce better query plans in some cases. This setting is disabled by default. [#140255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140255) [#140998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140998)
- Added the `optimizer_check_input_min_row_count` session setting to control the minimum row count estimate for buffer scans of foreign key and uniqueness checks. It defaults to `0`. [#141375](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141375)
- Since v23.2, table statistics histograms have been collected for non-indexed JSON columns. Histograms are no longer collected for these columns if the `sql.stats.non_indexed_json_histograms.enabled` cluster setting is set to `false`. This reduces memory usage during table statistics collection, for both automatic and manual collection via `ANALYZE` and `CREATE STATISTICS`. [#139897](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139897) [#140998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140998)
- Fixed a bug that could cause unexpected errors with SQL `VALUES` clauses that contain function calls with multiple overloads. This bug existed only in pre-release versions of v25.1. [#140646](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140646)
- Added the `optimizer_min_row_count` session setting. This setting sets a lower bound on row count estimates for relational expressions during query planning. A value of `0` (default) indicates no lower bound. If set to a value greater than `0`, a row count of zero can still be estimated for expressions with a cardinality of zero, e.g., for a contradictory filter. Setting this to a value greater than `0`, such as `1`, may yield better query plans in some cases, such as when statistics are frequently stale and inaccurate. [#140255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140255) [#140998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140998)

### Operational changes

- Reduced noise in dynamically provisioned logging sinks by logging flush errors at most once per minute. [#139643](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139643)
- The `cockroach node decommission` CLI command now waits until the target node is drained before marking it as fully decommissioned. Previously, it would start the drain but not wait, leaving the target node briefly in a state where it would be unable to communicate with the cluster but would still accept client requests (which would then hang or hit unexpected errors). [#139556](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139556)

### Command-line changes

- Improved the performance of the `cockroachd debug zip` command when retrieving data from `crdb_internal.transaction_contention_events`, reducing the likelihood of `memory budget exceeded` or `query execution canceled due to statement timeout` errors. [#139754](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139754)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, in changefeeds using CDC queries and the Parquet format, the output would include duplicate columns when it contained a user-defined primary key. Now, the columns are de-duplicated columns in the output when writing to Parquet. [#140153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140153)
- Fixed a bug where dropping a table with a trigger using the legacy schema changer could leave an orphaned reference in the descriptor. This occurred when two tables were dependent on each other via a trigger, and the table containing the trigger was dropped. [#141179](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141179)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `SHOW TABLES` and other introspection operations to encounter a `"batch timestamp must be after replica GC threshold"` error. [#140284](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140284)
- The Data Distribution and Zone Configs report on the DB Console Advanced Debug page will no longer crash if there are `NULL` values for the `raw_sql_config` column in the `crdb_internal.zones` table. [#140661](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140661)
- Fixed possible index corruption caused by triggers that could occur when the following conditions were satisfied:
    1. A query calls a user-defined function (UDF) or stored procedure, and also performs a mutation on a table.
    2. The UDF/stored procedure contains a statement that either fires an `AFTER` trigger, or fires a cascade that itself fires a trigger.
    3. The trigger modifies the same row as the outer statement.
    4. Either the outer or inner mutation is something other than an `INSERT` without an `ON CONFLICT` clause. [#138361](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138361)
- Fixed a bug where activating statement diagnostics sometimes appeared unresponsive, with no state or status update. The status now always indicates whether diagnostics are active or a statement bundle is available for download. [#139585](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139585)
- Fixed a memory leak that could previously occur when evaluating some memory-intensive queries via the vectorized engine in CockroachDB. The leak had been present since v20.2. [#139095](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139095)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `SHOW TABLES` and other introspection operations to encounter a `"batch timestamp must be after replica GC threshold"` error. [#140084](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140084)
- Fixed a bug in the `kafka_sink_config` option for changefeeds where users were previously unable to set negative GZIP compression levels. Users can now configure the `CompressionLevel` field in the range of `[-2, 9]` where `-2` enables Huffman encoding and `-1` sets the default compression. [#141037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141037)
- Fixed a bug that would cause an internal error when the result of a `RECORD` -returning user-defined function (UDF) was wrapped by another expression (such as `COALESCE` ) within a `VALUES` clause. [#140646](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140646)
- Fixed a rare bug in which a query could fail with the error `could not find computed column expression for column in table` while dropping a virtual computed column from a table. This bug was introduced in v23.2.4. [#139833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139833)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.5 on Github, visit [v24.3.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.4...v24.3.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.4...v24.3.5)

### General changes

- The protected timestamp records of running changefeeds are now updated when the set of targets changes, such as when system tables are added to the protected tables list. [#138654](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138654)

### Backward-incompatible changes

- In [v24.3.4](#v24-3-4-bug-fixes), a bug was fixed that could cause `SHOW TABLES` and other introspection operations to encounter a `"batch timestamp... must be after replica GC threshold"` error. This fix is **not** present in v24.3.5, but has been released in [v24.3.6](#v24-3-6). [#140175](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140175)

### SQL language changes

- Since v23.2 table statistics histograms have been collected for non-indexed JSON columns. Histograms are no longer collected for these columns if the `sql.stats.non_indexed_json_histograms.enabled` cluster setting is set to `false`. This reduces memory usage during table statistics collection, for both automatic and manual collection via `ANALYZE` and `CREATE STATISTICS`. [#140265](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140265)
- Added support for a new index hint, `AVOID_FULL_SCAN`, which will prevent the optimizer from planning a full scan for the specified table if any other plan is possible. The hint can be used in the same way as other existing index hints. For example, `SELECT * FROM table_name@{AVOID_FULL_SCAN};`. This hint is similar to `NO_FULL_SCAN`, but will not error if a full scan cannot be avoided. Note that normally a full scan of a partial index would not be considered a "full scan" for the purposes of the `NO_FULL_SCAN` and `AVOID_FULL_SCAN` hints, but if the user has explicitly forced the partial index via `FORCE_INDEX=index_name`, CockroachDB does consider it a full scan. [#140270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140270)
- Added the `optimizer_prefer_bounded_cardinality` session setting, which instructs the optimizer to prefer query plans where every expression has a guaranteed upper-bound on the number of rows it will process. This may help the optimizer produce better query plans in some cases. This setting is disabled by default. [#140270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140270)
- Added the `optimizer_min_row_count` session setting, which sets a lower bound on row count estimates for relational expressions during query planning. A value of zero, which is the default, indicates no lower bound. Note that if this is set to a value greater than zero, a row count of zero can still be estimated for expressions with a cardinality of zero, e.g., for a contradictory filter. Setting this to a value higher than `0`, such as `1`, may yield better query plans in some cases, such as when statistics are frequently stale and inaccurate. [#140270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140270)

### Operational changes

- Schema object identifiers (e.g., database names, schema names, table names, and function names) are no longer redacted when logging statements in the `EXEC` or `SQL_SCHEMA` channels. If redaction of these names is required, then the new cluster setting `sql.log.redact_names.enabled` can be set to `true`. The default value of the setting is `false`. [#138563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138563)
- Schema object identifiers (e.g., table names, schema names, function names, and type names) are no longer redacted in the `SQL_SCHEMA` log channel. [#138563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138563)
- Added the metric `sql.schema_changer.object_count`, which counts the number of objects in the cluster. [#138837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138837)
- The `changefeed.max_behind_nanos` metric now supports scoping with metrics labels. [#139234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139234)

### DB Console changes

- Added the `/debug/pprof/fgprof` endpoint to capture off-CPU stack traces. Use of this endpoint will have a noticable impact to performance while the endpoint is being triggered. [#138843](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138843)

### Bug fixes

- `CLOSE CURSOR` statements are now allowed in read-only transactions, similar to PostgreSQL. The bug had been present since at least v23.1. [#137793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137793)
- `ALTER BACKUP SCHEDULE` no longer fails on schedules whose collection URI contains a space. [#138082](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138082)
- Previously, `SHOW CREATE TABLE` was showing incorrect data for inverted indexes. It now shows the correct data that can be input to CockroachDB to recreate the same table. [#138083](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138083)
- Fixed a timing issue between `ALTER VIEW.. RENAME` and `DROP VIEW` that caused repeated failures in the `DROP VIEW` job. [#137889](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137889)
- Fixed a bug where querying the `pg_catalog.pg_constraint` table while the schema changer was dropping a constraint could result in a query error. [#137875](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137875)
- On the **Databases** page, users should no longer see console errors when visiting the **Databases** page directly after node/SQL pod startup. [#138377](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138377)
- In the **Databases** &gt; **Tables** page, the `CREATE` statement will now show up as expected for tables with custom schema names. [#138378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138378)
- Queries that perform a cast from the string representation of an array containing `GEOMETRY` or `GEOGRAPHY` types to a SQL `ARRAY` type will now succeed. [#138695](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138695)
- Previously, cluster backups taken in a multi-region cluster that had configured the system database with a region configuration could not be restored into a non-multi-region cluster. This is now fixed. [#138787](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138787)
- Fixed a bug that disregarded tuple labels in some cases. This could cause unexpected behavior, such as when converting a tuple to JSON with `to_jsonb`. See #136167 for more details. The incorrect removal of tuple labels bug was introduced in v22.1.0, and changes in v24.3.0 made unexpected behavior due to the bug more likely. [#138840](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138840)
- Previously, CockroachDB could encounter an internal error `comparison of two different versions of enum` in some cases when a user-defined type was modified within a transaction and the following statements read the column of that user-defined type. The bug was introduced in v24.2 and is now fixed. [#138052](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138052)
- Secondary tenants will no longer fatal when issuing HTTP requests during tenant startup. [#138755](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138755)
- Fixed a bug where columns created with `GENERATED... AS IDENTITY` with the `SERIAL` type could incorrectly fail internal validations. [#139101](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139101)
- When the session variable `allow_role_memberships_to_change_during_transaction` is set, it is now possible to create and drop users quickly even when there are contending transactions on the `system.users` and `system.role_options` system tables. [#139032](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139032)
- Fixed a bug where the error `batch timestamp... must be after replica GC threshold` could occur during a schema change backfill operation, and cause the schema change job to retry infinitely. Now this error is treated as permanent, and will cause the job to enter the `failed` state. [#139250](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139250)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the `CREATE` statement for a routine from being shown in a statement bundle. This happened when the routine was created on a schema other than `public`. The bug had existed since v23.1. [#136124](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136124)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.4 on Github, visit [v24.3.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.3...v24.3.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.3...v24.3.4)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause `SHOW TABLES` and other introspection operations to encounter a `"batch timestamp... must be after replica GC threshold"` error. [#140175](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140175)

<Warning>
This fix is present in v24.3.4 and [v24.3.6](#v24-3-6), but was **not** released in [v24.3.5](#v24-3-5).
</Warning>

Release Date: January 9, 2025

### Downloads

<Note>
