### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.3 on Github, visit [v24.3.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.2...v24.3.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.2...v24.3.3)

### General changes

- To improve the granularity of changefeed pipeline metrics, the changefeed metrics `changefeed.admit_latency` and `changefeed.commit_latency` have histogram buckets from `5ms` to `60m` (previously `500ms` to `5m` ). The following changefeed metrics have histogram buckets from `5ms` to `10m` (previously `500ms` to `5m` ):
    - `changefeed.parallel_io_queue_nanos`
    - `changefeed.parallel_io_result_queue_nanos`
    - `changefeed.sink_batch_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.flush_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.kafka_throttling_hist_nanos` [#136604](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136604)
- Added support for multiple seed brokers in the new Kafka sink. [#136727](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136727)
- Added a new metric `distsender.rangefeed.catchup_ranges_waiting_client_side` that counts how many rangefeeds are waiting on the client-side limiter to start performing catchup scans. [#136838](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136838)
- Added support for a new `AWS_USE_PATH_STYLE` parameter in S3 URI parsing. [#136934](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136934)

### SQL language changes

- Added support for `SHOW TRIGGERS`, which displays the names of all triggers on a table, and whether each trigger is enabled. The user must have any privilege on the table, or be its owner. [#135862](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135862)
- Added support for `SHOW CREATE TRIGGER`, which displays the CREATE statement for a trigger. The user must have any privilege on the table, or be its owner. [#135862](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135862)
- The names of `BEFORE` triggers fired by a mutation are now included in the `EXPLAIN` output, with the trigger-function invocations also visible in the output of verbose `EXPLAIN`. [#135864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135864)
- `AFTER` triggers are now included in the output of `EXPLAIN` and `EXPLAIN ANALYZE`. [#135864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135864)
- Added the `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting, which reverts the changes of [#133037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133037) that causes the change in typing behavior described in [#137837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137837). Specifically, it makes type-checking and overload resolution ignore the newly added "unpreferred" overloads. This setting defaults to `on`. [#137919](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137919)

### Operational changes

- Removed the `sql.auth.resolve_membership_single_scan.enabled` cluster setting. This was added out of precaution in case it was necessary to revert back to the old behavior for looking up role memberships, but this escape hatch has never been needed in practice since this was added in v23.1. [#136162](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136162)
- Telemetry delivery is now considered successful even in cases of a network timeout. This will prevent throttling in cases outside an operator's control. [#136480](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136480)
- When a schema change job is completed, rolls back, or encounters a failure, the time taken since the job began is now logged in a structured log in the `SQL_SCHEMA` log channel. [#136929](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136929)
- Added a new configurable parameter `kv.transaction.max_intents_and_locks` that will prevent transactions from creating too many intents. [#137687](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137687)
- Added the metric `txn.count_limit_rejected`, which tracks the KV transactions that have been aborted because they exceeded the max number of writes and locking reads allowed. [#137687](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137687)
- Added the metric `txn.count_limit_on_response`, which tracks the number of KV transactions that have exceeded the count limit on a response. [#137687](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137687)

### DB Console changes

- The link on the Plan Details page to the legacy Table page has been removed. [#136504](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136504)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, CockroachDB would encounter an internal error when evaluating `FETCH ABSOLUTE 0` statements, and this is now fixed. The bug has been present since v22.1. [#134995](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134995)
- Fixed an issue where corrupted table statistics could cause the `cockroach` process to crash. [#136042](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136042)
- A table that is participating in a logical replication stream can no longer be dropped. Previously this was allowed, which would cause all the replicated rows to end up in the dead-letter queue. [#136255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136255)
- `ALTER COLUMN SET NOT NULL` was not enforced consistently when the table was created in the same transaction. [#136323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136323)
- Fixed a bug where `CREATE RELATION / TYPE` could leave dangling namespace entries if the schema was concurrently being dropped. [#136378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136378)
- `security.certificate.*` metrics will now be updated if a node loads new certificates while running. [#136226](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136226)
- The `idle_in_session_timeout` setting now excludes the time spent waiting for schema changer jobs to complete, preventing unintended session termination during schema change operations. [#136490](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136490)
- Fixed a bug that causes the optimizer to use stale table statistics after altering an `ENUM` type used in the table. [#136630](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136630)
- Changes the table, index contents of the hot ranges page in DB console. [#134988](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134988)
- Table statistics collection in CockroachDB could previously run into `no bytes in account to release` errors in some edge cases (when the SQL memory budget, configured via `--max-sql-memory` flag, was close to being exhausted). The bug has been present since v21.2 and is now fixed. [#136166](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136166)
- CockroachDB now better respects `statement_timeout` limit on queries involving the top K sort and merge join operations. [#136653](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136653)
- Fixed an issue where license enforcement was not consistently disabled for single-node clusters started with `cockroach start-single-node`. The fix ensures proper behavior on cluster restarts. [#137012](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137012)
- Fixed a bug that caused queries against tables with user-defined types to sometimes fail with errors after restoring those tables. [#137353](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137353)
- Fixed a bug that causes an incorrect filesystem to be logged as part of the store information. [#137115](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137115)
- Fixed a bug affecting uniqueness enforcement in regional by row tables when using read-committed isolation. The bug, introduced in v24.3.0, could cause internal errors or incorrect uniqueness enforcement in tables that had both non-unique and unique indexes when the region column was not part of the uniqueness constraints. [#137366](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137366)
- Fixed a bug that has existed since v24.1 that would cause a set-returning UDF with `OUT` parameters to return a single row. [#137376](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137376)
- Fixed an issue where adding an existing column with the `IF NOT EXISTS` option could exit too early, skipping necessary handling of the abstract syntax tree (AST). This could lead to failure of the `ALTER` statement. [#137675](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137675)
- An issue where a schema change could incorrectly cause a changefeed to fail with an assertion error like `received boundary timestamp... of type... before reaching existing boundary of type...` has now been fixed. [#137706](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137706)
- Internal scans are now exempt from the `sql.defaults.disallow_full_table_scans.enabled` setting, allowing index creation even when the cluster setting is active. [#137725](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137725)
- The `pg_catalog.pg_type` table no longer contains `NULL` values for the columns `typinput`, `typoutput`, `typreceive`, and `typsend`. `NULL` values were erroneously added for these columns for the `trigger` type in v24.3.0. This could cause unexpected errors with some client libraries. [#137941](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137941)

### Performance improvements

- Improved the internal caching logic for role membership information. This reduces the latency impact of commands such as `DROP ROLE`, `CREATE ROLE`, and `GRANT role TO user`, which cause the role membership cache to be invalidated. [#136162](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136162)

## v24.3.2

Release Date: December 26, 2024

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.2 on Github, visit [v24.3.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.1...v24.3.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.1...v24.3.2)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting. When set to `on`, type-checking comparisons involving `VARCHAR` columns behave as they did in all previous versions. When set to `off`, type-checking of these comparisons is more strict and queries that previously succeeded may now error with the message `unsupported comparison operator`. These errors can be fixed by adding explicit type casts. The `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting is on by default. [#137943](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137943)

Release Date: December 12, 2024

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.3.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.1 on Github, visit [v24.3.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0...v24.3.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0...v24.3.1)

### SQL language changes

- When triggers fire one another cyclically, the new `recursion_depth_limit` setting now limits the depth of the recursion. By default, the limit is `1000` nested trigger executions. [#135046](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135046)

### Operational changes

- The metrics scrape HTTP endpoint at `/ _status/vars` will now truncate HELP text at the first sentence, reducing the metadata for metrics with large descriptions. Customers can still access these descriptions via our docs. [#135021](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135021)
- The row-level TTL job now periodically updates the progress meter in the jobs introspection interfaces, including `SHOW JOBS` and the Jobs page in the DB console. [#135171](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135171)
- Telemetry delivery is now considered successful even in cases where we experience a network timeout. This will prevent throttling in cases outside an operator's control. [#136481](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136481)

### DB Console changes

- When activating statement diagnostics in the DB Console, users now have the option to produce a redacted bundle as output. This bundle will omit sensitive data. [#134993](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134993)

### Other changes

- Protected timestamp records for changefeeds now include the `system.users` table. This ensures that user information remains available when running CDC queries against historical data. [#134238](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134238)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause `DELETE` triggers not to fire on cascading delete, and which could cause `INSERT` triggers to match incorrectly in the same scenario. [#134896](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134896)
- Reduced the duration of partitions in the gossip network when a node crashes in order to eliminate false positives in the `ranges.unavailable` metric. [#134480](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134480)
- When a non-admin user runs `DROP ROLE IF EXISTS` on a user that does not exist, an error is no longer returned. [#134970](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134970)
- Fixed a bug that could cause incorrect query results when the optimizer planned a lookup join on an index containing a column of type `CHAR(N)`, `VARCHAR(N)`, `BIT(N)`, `VARBIT(N)`, or `DECIMAL(M, N)`, and the query held that column constant to a single value (e.g. with an equality filter). [#135037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135037)
- Fixed an unhandled error that would occur if `DROP SCHEMA` was executed on the `public` schema of the `system` database, or on an internal schema like `pg_catalog` or `information_schema`. [#135181](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135181)
- A bug has been fixed that caused incorrect evaluation of some binary expressions involving `CHAR(N)` values and untyped string literals with trailing whitespace characters. For example, the expression `'f'::CHAR = 'f '` now correctly evaluates to `true`. [#134710](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134710)
- Prevent `ALTER DATABASE` operations that modify the zone config from hanging if an invalid zone config already exists. [#135216](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135216)
- `CREATE SCHEMA` now returns the correct error if a schema name is missing. [#135928](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135928)
- `percentile_cont` and `percentile_disc` aggregate functions now support `float4` data type inputs. Previously, these functions would return an error when used with `float4` values. [#135764](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135764)
- `security.certificate.*` metrics now update correctly when certificates are reloaded during node runtime. Previously, these metrics would not reflect changes to certificates after node startup. [#136227](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136227)
- SQL roles created from LDAP groups that contain periods (.) or hyphens (-) in their Common Names (CN) no longer result in authorization failures. [#134942](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134942)
- LDAP authorization now supports partial group mapping, allowing users to authenticate even when some LDAP groups do not have corresponding CockroachDB roles. Previously, authentication would fail if any LDAP group lacked a matching database role. [#135587](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135587)
- Regional by row tables with uniqueness constraints where the region is not part of those uniqueness constraints and which also contain non-unique indices will now have those constraints properly enforced when modified at `READ COMMITTED` isolation. This bug was introduced in v24.3.0. [#137367](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137367)

### Performance improvements

- The `_status/nodes_ui` API no longer returns unnecessary metrics in its response. This decreases the payload size of the API and improves the load time of various DB Console pages and components. [#135209](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135209)
- PL/pgSQL loops now execute up to 3-4x faster through improved optimization, particularly when they contain subqueries. This enhancement improves performance for routines with many iterations or nested operations. [#135648](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135648)

#### Disaster Recovery

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="5" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Advanced</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Standard</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Basic</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>SELECT now supported on PCR standby clusters<br/><br/><a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/physical-cluster-replication-overview">Physical cluster replication (PCR)</a> has been enhanced to support <code>SELECT</code> operations on standby clusters. This enables you to scale read performance by running, for example, non-critical workloads on standby clusters.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Logical Data Replication in Preview<br/><br/><a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/logical-data-replication-overview">Logical data replication (LDR)</a> continuously replicates tables between an active source CockroachDB cluster to an active destination CockroachDB cluster. Both source and destination can receive application reads and writes, and participate in bidirectional LDR replication for eventual consistency in the replicating tables.<br/><br/>The active-active setup between clusters can provide protection against cluster, datacenter, or region failure while still achieving single-region low latency reads and writes in the individual CockroachDB clusters. Each cluster in an LDR job still benefits individually from multi-active availability with CockroachDB's built-in Raft replication providing data consistency across nodes, zones, and regions.<br/><br/>This feature is in Preview.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

#### SQL

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="5" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Advanced</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Standard</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Basic</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>User-defined functions and stored procedures support SECURITY DEFINER<br/><br/>You can create or alter a <a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/user-defined-functions">user-defined function (UDF)</a> or <a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/stored-procedures">stored procedure</a> with <code>&#91;EXTERNAL&#93; SECURITY DEFINER</code> instead of the default <code>&#91;EXTERNAL&#93; SECURITY INVOKER</code>. With <a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/create-function#create-a-security-definer-function"><code>&#91;SECURITY DEFINER&#93;</code></a>, the privileges of the owner are checked when the UDF or stored procedure is executed, rather than the privileges of the executor. The <code>EXTERNAL</code> keyword is optional and exists for SQL language conformity.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>CockroachDB now supports triggers in Preview<br/><br/>CockroachDB now supports <a href="https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.3/triggers">triggers</a>. Triggers allow automatic execution of specified functions in response to specified events on a particular table or view. They can be used for automating tasks, enforcing business rules, and maintaining data integrity. This feature is in Preview.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

#### Security

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="5" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Advanced</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Standard</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Basic</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>LDAP support in Preview<br/><br/>CockroachDB supports <a href="/docs/v24.3/ldap-authentication">authentication and authorization using LDAP-compatible directory services</a>, such as Active Directory and Microsoft Entra ID. #### Observability

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="5" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Advanced</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Standard</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Basic</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Improved usability for the DB Console Metrics page<br/><br/>Introduced several enhancements to the DB Console Metrics page to support large scale clusters, including the following:<br/><br/>- Added on-hover cursor support that will display the closest time-series value and highlight the node in the legend to allow users to quickly pinpoint outliers.<br/><br/>- Improved legend visibillity and made legends scrollable to improve usability and reduce vertical scrolling.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Improved peformance and scalability for the DB Console Databases pages<br/><br/>CockroachDB now caches the data that is surfaced in the Databases page. This enhances the performance and scalability of the Databases page for large-scale clusters.</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Improved admission control observability<br/><br/>The DB Console Overload page now provides additional metrics to help identify overload in the system. Graphs and metrics on this page provide quick signals on which resource is exhausted and whether it is due to background activity or foreground.<br/><br/>There are now 4 graphs for admission queue delay:<br/><br/>1. Foreground (regular) CPU work<br/><br/>2. Store (IO) work<br/><br/>3. Background (elastic) CPU work<br/><br/>4. Replication admission control (store overload on replicas)</td><td>24.3</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

<table><thead><tr><th colspan="2" id="feature-detail-key">Feature detail key</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>★</td><td>Features marked "All&#42;" were recently made available in the CockroachDB Cloud platform. They are available for all supported versions of CockroachDB, under the deployment methods specified in their row under Availability.</td></tr><tr><td>★★</td><td>Features marked "All&#42;&#42;" were recently made available via tools maintained outside of the CockroachDB binary. #### Backward-incompatible changes

Before <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrading to CockroachDB v24.3</a>, be sure to review the following backward-incompatible changes, as well as [key cluster setting changes](#v24-3-0-cluster-settings), and adjust your deployment as necessary.

If you plan to upgrade to v24.3 directly from v24.1 and skip v24.2, be sure to also review the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v24.2" data-versioned="true">v24.2 release notes</a> for backward-incompatible changes from v24.1.

- Upgrading to v24.3 is blocked if no <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs" data-versioned="true">license</a> is installed, or if a trial/free license is installed with telemetry disabled. [#130576](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130576)

#### Features that Require Upgrade Finalization

During a major-version upgrade, certain features and performance improvements may not be available until the upgrade is finalized.

- A cluster must have an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs#set-a-license" data-versioned="true">Enterprise license</a> or a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs#obtain-a-license" data-versioned="true">trial license</a> set before an upgrade to v24.3 can be finalized.
- New clusters that are initialized for the first time on v24.3, and clusters that are upgraded to v24.3 will now have a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones" data-versioned="true">zone config</a> defined for the `timeseries` range if it does not already exist, which specifies the value for `gc.ttlseconds`, but inherits all other attributes from the zone config for the `default` range.

#### Key Cluster Setting Changes

Changes to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> should be reviewed prior to upgrading. New default cluster setting values will be used unless you have manually set a value for a setting. This can be confirmed by running the SQL statement `SELECT * FROM system.settings` to view the non-default settings.

- [Settings added](#v24-3-0-settings-added)
- [Settings with changed defaults](#v24-3-0-settings-with-changed-defaults)
- [Settings with changed visibility](#v24-3-0-settings-with-changed-visibility)
- [Additional setting changes](#v24-3-0-additional-cluster-setting-changes)

##### Settings added

- `goschedstats.always_use_short_sample_period.enabled`: when set to `true`, helps to prevent unnecessary queueing due to CPU <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> by forcing `1ms` sampling of runnable queue lengths. The default value is `false`. [#133585](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133585)
- `kv.range.range_size_hard_cap`: allows you to limit how large a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">range</a> can grow before <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#split-failed-while-applying-backpressure-are-rows-updated-in-a-tight-loop" data-versioned="true">backpressure</a> is applied. This can help to mitigate against a situation where a range cannot be split, such as when a range is comprised of a single key due to an issue with the schema or workload pattern, or a bug in client application code. The default is `8 GiB`, 16 times the default maximum range size. If you have changed the maximum range size, you may need to adjust this cluster setting or reduce the range size. [#129450](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129450)
- `kvadmission.flow_controller.token_reset_epoch`: can be used to refill replication <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> v2 tokens. This setting is marked as `reserved`, as it is not supported for tuning, by default. Use it only after consultation with your account team. [#133294](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133294)
- `kvadmission.store.snapshot_ingest_bandwidth_control.enabled`: enables a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">Admission Control</a> integration for pacing snapshot ingest traffic based on disk bandwidth. It requires provisioned bandwidth to be set for the store, or the cluster through the setting `kvadmission.store.provisioned_bandwidth`, for it to take effect. [#131243](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131243)
- Settings have been added which control the refresh behavior for the cached data in the Databases page of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>:
    - `obs.tablemetadatacache.data_valid_duration`: the duration for which the data in `system.table_metadata` is considered valid before a cache reset will occur. Default: 20 minutes.
    - `obs.tablemetadatacache.automatic_updates.enabled`: whether to automatically update the cache according the validity interval. Default: `false`.

        [#130198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130198)
- `server.jwt_authentication.client.timeout`: the HTTP client timeout for external calls made during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">JWT authentication</a>. [#127145](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127145)
- Partial <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> can now be automatically collected at the extremes of indexes when a certain fraction and minimum number of rows are stale (by default 5% and 100%, respectively). These can be configured with new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-and-reset-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">table storage parameters</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>:
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.enabled` (table parameter `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_enabled` ) - both default to `false`.
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.min_stale_rows` (table parameter `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_min_stale_rows` ) - both default to `100`.
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.fraction_stale_rows` (table parameter `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_fraction_stale_rows` ) - both default to `0.05`.

        [#93067](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93067)
- `sql.stats.histogram_buckets.include_most_common_values.enabled`: controls whether common values are included in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#control-histogram-collection" data-versioned="true">histogram collection</a> for use by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a>. When enabled, histogram buckets will represent the most common sampled values as upper bounds. [#129378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129378)
- `sql.stats.histogram_buckets.max_fraction_most_common_values`: controls the fraction of buckets that can be adjusted to include common values. Defaults to `0.1`. [#129378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129378)
- `sql.txn.repeatable_read_isolation.enabled`: defaults to `false`. When set to `true`, the following statements configure transactions to run under `REPEATABLE READ` isolation, rather than being automatically interpreted as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/demo-serializable" data-versioned="true">`SERIALIZABLE`</a>:
    - `BEGIN TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`
    - `SET TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`
    - `SET default_transaction_isolation = 'repeatable read'`
    - `SET SESSION CHARACTERISTICS AS TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`

##### Settings with changed defaults

- The default for `sql.defaults.large_full_scan_rows` is now `0`. If a user is using session var values inherited from these settings, when `sql.defaults.disallow_full_table_scans.enabled` is set to `true`: all full table scans are now disallowed by default, even full scans on very small tables, but if `sql.defaults.large_full_scan_rows` is set to a number greater than `0`, full scans are allowed if they are estimated to read fewer than that number of rows.
    - **Note:** All `sql.defaults` settings are maintained for backward compatibility. We recommend using `ALTER ROLE`, instead, to set the corresponding session vars for users (in this case, `large_full_scan_rows` and `disallow_full_table_scans` ). For more information, see the note on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#settings" data-versioned="true">Cluster Settings table</a>.
- Increased the per-vCPU concurrency limits for KV operations:
    - The default for `kv.dist_sender.concurrency_limit` (reserved) has changed from `64` per vCPU to `384` per vCPU. (In v24.3, it is possible to estimate the current concurrency level using the new metric `distsender.batches.async.in_progress`.)
    - The default for `kv.streamer.concurrency_limit` (reserved) has changed from `8` per vCPU to `96` per vCPU.
    - These are `reserved` settings, not intended for tuning by customers.
    - When running `SHOW CLUSTER SETTING`, the displayed setting values will depend on the node's number of vCPUs.
    - Contact Support if the number of `distsender.batches.async.throttled` requests is persistently greater than zero.

        [#131226](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131226)
- The default for `server.oidc_authentication.client.timeout`, which sets the client timeout for external calls made during OIDC authentication, has changed from `30s` to `15s`.

##### Settings with changed visibility

The following settings are now marked `public` after previously being `reserved`. Reserved settings are not documented and their tuning by customers is not supported.

- Cluster settings for configuring <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup#cluster-settings-for-cloud-storage" data-versioned="true">rate limiting for traffic to cloud storage</a> are now public.
    - These settings have the prefix `cloudstorage` followed by:
        1. a provider or protocol ( `azure`, `gs`, `s3`, `http`, `nodelocal`, `userfile`, or `nullsink` )
        2. `read` or `write`
        3. `node_burst_limit` or `node_rate_limit`
    - For example, `cloudstorage.s3.write.node_burst_limit`. [#127207](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127207)
- JWT authentication have been made `public`. [#128170](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128170)
    - `server.jwt_authentication.audience`
    - `server.jwt_authentication.claim`
    - `server.jwt_authentication.enabled`
    - `server.jwt_authentication.issuers.custom_ca`
    - `server.jwt_authentication.jwks`
    - `server.jwt_authentication.jwks_auto_fetch.enabled`
- Settings with the prefix `server.ldap_authentication` have been made `public` with the Preview release of LDAP support:
    - `server.ldap_authentication.client.tls_certificate`
    - `server.ldap_authentication.client.tls_key`
    - `server.ldap_authentication.domain.custom_ca`

##### Additional cluster setting changes

- The setting `server.host_based_authentication.configuration` now supports LDAP configuration, and its value is now redacted for non-admin users when the `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` is set to `true`. [#131150](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131150)
- The settings <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-enterprise-license" data-versioned="true">`enterprise.license`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-diagnostics-reporting-enabled" data-versioned="true">`diagnostics.reporting.enabled`</a> now have additional validation. To disable diagnostics reporting, the cluster must also have a license that is not an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs#types-of-licenses" data-versioned="true">Enterprise Trial or Enterprise Free license</a>. Additionally, to set one of these licenses, the cluster must already be submitting diagnostics information. [#131097](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131097) [#132257](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132257)
- `sql.defaults.vectorize` now supports the value `1` (in addition to `0` and `2`) to indicate `on`, to address a bug that could cause new connections to fail after an upgrade with a message referencing an `invalid value for parameter "vectorize": "unknown(1)"`. [#133371](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133371)
- The description of the setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-sink-io-workers" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.sink_io_workers`</a> has been updated to reflect all of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">sinks</a> that support the setting: the batching versions of webhook, pubsub, and kafka sinks that are enabled by `changefeed.new_<sink type>_sink_enabled`. [#129946](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129946)

#### Deprecations

The following deprecations are announced in v24.3. If you plan to upgrade to v24.3 directly from v24.1 and skip v24.2, be sure to also review the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v24.2" data-versioned="true">v24.2 release notes</a> for deprecations.

- The session variable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#enforce-home-region-follower-reads-enabled" data-versioned="true">`enforce_home_region_follower_reads_enabled`</a> is now deprecated, and will be removed in a future release. The related session variable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#enforce-home-region" data-versioned="true">`enforce_home_region`</a> is **not** deprecated. [#129024](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129024)

#### Known limitations

For information about new and unresolved limitations in CockroachDB v24.3, with suggested workarounds where applicable, refer to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/known-limitations" data-versioned="true">Known Limitations</a>.

You will learn what differentiates CockroachDB from both legacy SQL and NoSQL databases and how CockroachDB ensures consistent transactions without sacrificing scale and resiliency. You'll learn about CockroachDB's seamless horizontal scalability, distributed transactions with strict ACID guarantees, and high availability and resilience.</td></tr><tr><td>Cockroach University</td><td><a href="https://university.cockroachlabs.com/courses/course-v1:crl+practical-first-steps-with-crdb+self-paced/about">Practical First Steps with CockroachDB</a></td><td>This course will give you the tools you need to get started with CockroachDB. During the course, you will learn how to spin up a cluster, use the Admin UI to monitor cluster activity, and use SQL shell to solve a set of hands-on exercises.</td></tr><tr><td>Cockroach University</td><td><a href="https://university.cockroachlabs.com/courses/course-v1:crl+client-side-txn-handling+self-paced/about">Enterprise Application Development with CockroachDB</a></td><td>This course is the first in a series designed to equip you with best practices for mastering application-level (client-side) transaction management in CockroachDB. We'll dive deep on common differences between CockroachDB and legacy SQL databases and help you sidestep challenges you might encounter when migrating to CockroachDB from Oracle, PostgreSQL, and MySQL.</td></tr><tr><td>Cockroach University</td><td><a href="https://university.cockroachlabs.com/courses/course-v1:crl+intro-to-resilience-in-multi-region+self-paced/about">Building a Highly Resilient Multi-region Database using CockroachDB</a></td><td>This course is part of a series introducing solutions to running low-latency, highly resilient applications for data-intensive workloads on CockroachDB. In this course we focus on surviving large-scale infrastructure failures like losing an entire cloud region without losing data during recovery. We'll show you how to use CockroachDB survival goals in a multi-region cluster to implement a highly resilient database that survives node or network failures across multiple regions with zero data loss.</td></tr><tr><td>Docs</td><td><a href="/docs/molt/migration-overview">Migration Overview</a></td><td>This page summarizes the steps of migrating a database to CockroachDB, which include testing and updating your schema to work with CockroachDB, moving your data into CockroachDB, and testing and updating your application.</td></tr><tr><td>Docs</td><td><a href="/docs/v24.3/architecture/overview">Architecture Overview</a></td><td>This page provides a starting point for understanding the architecture and design choices that enable CockroachDB's scalability and consistency capabilities.</td></tr><tr><td>Docs</td><td><a href="/docs/v24.3/sql-feature-support">SQL Feature Support</a></td><td>The page summarizes the standard SQL features CockroachDB supports as well as common extensions to the standard.</td></tr><tr><td>Docs</td><td><a href="/docs/v24.3/change-data-capture-overview">Change Data Capture Overview</a></td><td>This page summarizes CockroachDB's data streaming capabilities. Change data capture (CDC) provides efficient, distributed, row-level changefeeds into a configurable sink for downstream processing such as reporting, caching, or full-text indexing.</td></tr><tr><td>Docs</td><td><a href="/docs/v24.3/backup-architecture">Backup Architecture</a></td><td>This page describes the backup job workflow with a high-level overview, diagrams, and more details on each phase of the job.</td></tr></tbody></table>

Release Date: November 18, 2024

</Warning>

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-rc.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-rc.1 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-rc.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-rc.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0-beta.3...v24.3.0-rc.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0-beta.3...v24.3.0-rc.1)

### Security updates

- All cluster settings that accept strings are now fully redacted when transmitted as part of CockroachDB's diagnostics telemetry. This payload includes a record of modified cluster settings and their values when they are not strings. Customers who previously applied the mitigations in Technical Advisory 133479 can safely set the value of cluster setting `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` to false and turn on diagnostic reporting via the `diagnostics.reporting.enabled` cluster setting without leaking sensitive cluster settings values. [#134018](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134018)

### SQL language changes

- Row-level `AFTER` triggers can now be executed in response to mutations on a table. Row-level `AFTER` triggers fire after checks and cascades have completed for the query. [#133320](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133320)
- Cascades can now execute row-level `BEFORE` triggers. By default, attempting to modify or eliminate the cascading `UPDATE` or `DELETE` operation results in a `Triggered Data Change Violation` error. To bypass this error, you can set the `unsafe_allow_triggers_modifying_cascades` query option to `true`. This could result in constraint violations. [#134444](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134444)
- String constants can now be compared with collated strings. [#134086](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134086)

### Operational changes

- The `kvadmission.low_pri_read_elastic_control.enabled` cluster setting has been removed, because all bulk requests are now subject to elastic admission control admission by default. [#134486](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134486)
- The following metrics have been added for Logic Data Replication (LDR):
    - `logical_replication.catchup_ranges`: the number of source side ranges conducting catchup scans.
    - `logical_replication.scanning_ranges`: the number source side ranges conducting initial scans.
    - In the DB Console, these metrics may not be accurate if multiple LDR jobs are running. The metrics are accurate when exported from the Prometheus endpoint. [#134674](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134674)
- The backup and restore syntax update of `cockroach workload` which was introduced in [#134610](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134610) #has been reverted. [#134645](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134645)

### DB Console changes

- After finalizing an upgrade to v24.3, an updated version of the **Databases** page will be available. [#134244](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134244)
- Users with the `CONNECT` privilege can now access the **Databases** page. [#134542](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134542)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where an LDAP connection would be closed by the server and would not be retried by CockroachDB. [#134277](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134277)
- Fixed a bug that prevented LDAP authorization from successfully assigning CockroachDB roles to users when the source group name contained periods or hyphens. [#134944](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134944)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 that could cause significantly increased query latency while executing queries with index or lookup joins when the ordering needs to be maintained [#134367](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134367)
- Fixed a bug where `UPSERT` statements on regional by row tables under non-serializable isolations would not display show uniqueness constraints in `EXPLAIN` output. Even when not displayed, the constraints were enforced. [#134267](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134267)
- Fixed a bug where uniqueness constraints constraints enforced with tombstone writes were not shown in the output of `EXPLAIN (OPT)`. [#134482](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134482)
- Fixed a bug where `DISCARD ALL` statements were erroneously counted under the `sql.ddl.count` metric instead of the `sql.misc.count` metric. [#134510](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134510)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a backup or restore operation on AWS to fail with a KMS error due to a missing `default` shared config. [#134536](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134536)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent a user from running schema change operations on a restored table that was previously apart of a Logic Data Replication (LDR) stream. [#134675](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134675)

### Performance improvements

- The optimizer now generates more efficient query plans involving inverted indexes for queries with a conjunctive filter on the same JSON or ARRAY column. For example:

    ```sql
    SELECT * FROM t WHERE j->'a' = '10' AND j->'b' = '20'
    ```

    [#134002](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134002)

### Build changes

- Upgraded to Go 1.22.8 [#134427](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134427)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-beta.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-beta.3 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-beta.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-beta.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0-beta.2...v24.3.0-beta.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0-beta.2...v24.3.0-beta.3)

### Security updates

- Client authentication errors using LDAP now log more details to help with troubleshooting authentication and authorization issues. [#133812](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133812)

### SQL changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">Physical Cluster Replication</a> reader catalogs now bypass AOST timestamps using the `bypass_pcr_reader_catalog_aost` session variable, which can be used to modify cluster settings within the reader. [#133876](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133876)

### Operational changes

- Added a timer for inner <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sink</a> client flushes. [#133288](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133288)
- Rows replicated by Logical Data Replication in `immediate` mode are now considered in the decision to recompute SQL table statistics. [#133591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133591)
- The new cluster setting `kvadmission.flow_controller.token_reset_epoch` can be used to refill replication <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> v2 tokens. This is an advanced setting. Use it only after consultation with your account team. [#133294](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133294)
- The new cluster setting `goschedstats.always_use_short_sample_period.enabled`, when set to `true`, helps to prevent unnecessary queueing due to CPU [admission control](/docs/v24.3/admission-control.htmls. [#133585](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133585)

### DB Console changes

- In <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Database</a> pages, the **Refresh** tooltip now includes details about the progress of cache updates and when the job started. [#133351](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133351)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sink</a> ) timers were not correctly registered with the metric system. [#133288](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133288)
- Fixed a bug that could cause new connections to fail with the following error after upgrading: `ERROR: invalid value for parameter "vectorize": "unknown(1)" SQLSTATE: 22023 HINT: Available values: off,on,experimental_always`. To encounter this bug, the cluster must have:
    1. Run on version v21.1 at some point in the past
    2. Run `SET CLUSTER SETTING sql.defaults.vectorize = 'on';` while running v21.1.
    3. **Not** set `sql.defaults.vectorize` after upgrading past v21.1 4.
    4. Subsequently upgraded to v24.2.upgraded all the way to v24.2.

        To detect this bug, run the following query:

        ```sql
        SELECT * FROM system.settings WHERE name = 'sql.defaults.vectorize
        ```

        If the command returns `1` instead of `on`, run the following statement before upgrading.

        ```sql
        RESET CLUSTER SETTING sql.defaults.vectorize;
        ```

        `1` is now allowed as a value for this setting, and is equivalent to `on`. [#133371](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133371)
- Fixed a bug in v22.2.13+, v23.1.9+, and v23.2 that could cause the internal error `interface conversion: coldata.Column is` in an edge case. [#133762](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133762)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v20.1.0 that could cause erroneous `NOT NULL` constraint violation errors to be logged during `UPSERT` and `INSERT` statements with the `ON CONFLICT...DO UPDATE` clause that update an existing row and a subset of columns that did not include a `NOT NULL` column of the table. [#133820](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133820)
- Fixed a that could cache and reuse a non-reusable query plan, such as a plan for a DDL or `SHOW` statement, when `plan_cache_mode` was set to `auto` or `force_generic_plan`, which are not the default options. [#133073](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133073)
- Fixed an unhandled error that could occur while running the command `REVOKE... ON SEQUENCE FROM... {user}` on an object that is not a sequence. [#133710](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133710)
- Fixed a panic that could occur while running a `CREATE TABLE AS` statement that included a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">sequence</a> with an invalid function overload. [#133870](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133870)

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>ARM</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>Windows<br/>(Experimental)</td><td>Intel</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.3.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-beta.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-beta.2 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-beta.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-beta.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0-beta.1...v24.3.0-beta.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0-beta.1...v24.3.0-beta.2)

### SQL language changes

- If a table is the destination of a logical data replication stream, then only schema change statements that are deemed safe are allowed on the table. Safe statements are those that do not result in a rebuild of the primary <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> and do not create an index on a virtual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a>. [#133266](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133266)

### Operational changes

- The two new metrics `sql.crud_query.count` and `sql.crud_query.started.count` measure the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> / <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> / <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> / <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries" data-versioned="true">`SELECT`</a> queries executed and started respectively. [#133198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133198)
- When creating a logical data replication stream, any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined types</a> in the source and destination are now checked for equivalency. This allows for creating a stream that handles user-defined types without needing to use the `WITH SKIP SCHEMA CHECK` option as long as the stream uses `mode = immediate`. [#133274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133274)
- Logical data replication streams that reference tables with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined types</a> can now be created with the `mode = immediate` option. [#133295](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133295)

### DB Console changes

- The **SQL Statements** graph on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Overview**</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**SQL**</a> dashboard pages in DB Console has been renamed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard#sql-queries-per-second" data-versioned="true">**SQL Queries Per Second**</a> and now shows **Total Queries** as a general Queries Per Second (QPS) metric. [#133198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133198)
- Due to the inaccuracy of the **Range Count** column on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a> and the cost incurred to fetch the correct range count for every database in a cluster, this data will no longer be visible. This data is still available via a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW RANGES`</a> query. [#133267](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133267)

### Bug fixes

- Users with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">`admin` role</a> can now run <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-default-privileges" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR target_role...`</a> on any `target_role`. Previously, this could result in a privilege error, which is incorrect as `admin` s are allowed to perform any operation. [#133072](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133072)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/reassign-owned" data-versioned="true">`REASSIGN OWNED BY current_owner_role...`</a> will now transfer ownership of the `public` schema. Previously, it would always skip over the `public` schema even if it was owned by the `current_owner_role`. [#133072](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133072)

## v24.3.0-beta.1

Release Date: October 24, 2024

### Downloads

<Warning>
CockroachDB v24.3.0-beta.1 is a testing release. Testing releases are intended for testing and experimentation only, and are not qualified for production environments and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
</Warning>

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-beta.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-beta.1 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-beta.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-beta.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0-alpha.2...v24.3.0-beta.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0-alpha.2...v24.3.0-beta.1)

### General changes

- The cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-diagnostics-reporting-enabled" data-versioned="true">`diagnostics.reporting.enabled`</a> is now ignored if the cluster has a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs#types-of-licenses" data-versioned="true">Enterprise Trial or Enterprise Free license</a>, or if the reporting job is unable to load any license at all. [#132257](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132257)

### Enterprise edition changes

- This change ensures authorization with LDAP only works when the `ldapgrouplistfilter` option is present in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authentication#hba-configuration-syntax" data-versioned="true">HBA configuration</a>, otherwise authentication will proceed with the provided LDAP auth method options in the HBA configuration. This change is to ensure external authorization with LDAP is opt-in rather than enabled by default. [#132235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132235)
- Added a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sink</a> error metric `changefeed.sink_errors`, and expanded reporting of the internal retries metric `changefeed.internal_retry_message_count` to all sinks that perform internal retries. [#132092](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132092)

### SQL language changes

- Implemented `DROP TRIGGER` statements. The `CASCADE` option for dropping a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-feature-support" data-versioned="true">trigger</a> is not supported. [#128540](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128540)
- Added support for `CREATE TRIGGER`. The `OR REPLACE` syntax is not supported. Also, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-feature-support" data-versioned="true">triggers</a> cannot be executed, so creation is a no-op. [#128540](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128540)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partitioning" data-versioned="true">`PARTITION ALL BY`</a> tables can now be inserted into under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">non-`SERIALIZABLE` isolation levels</a> as long as there is no `ON CONFLICT` clause in the statement. Also, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partitioning" data-versioned="true">`PARTITION ALL BY`</a> tables can now be updated under non- `SERIALIZABLE` isolation levels. [#129837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129837)
- Attempting to add <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign keys</a> referencing a table with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> enabled will generate a notice informing the user about potential impact on the row-level TTL deletion job. Similarly, a notice is generated while attempting to enable row-level TTL on a table that has inbound foreign key references. [#127935](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127935)
- It is now possible to assign to an element of a composite typed variable in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a>. For example, given a variable `foo` with two integer elements `x` and `y`, the following assignment statement is allowed: `foo.x:= 100;`. [#132628](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132628)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">Backup</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> now work for tables with triggers. When the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore#skip-missing-udfs" data-versioned="true">`skip_missing_udfs` option</a> is applied, triggers with missing trigger functions are removed from the table. [#128555](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128555)
- `UPSERT and INSERT... ON CONFLICT` statements are now supported on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED` isolation</a>. [#132768](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132768)
- Added support for row-level `BEFORE` triggers. A row-level trigger executes the trigger function for each row that is being mutated. `BEFORE` triggers fire before the mutation operation. [#132511](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132511)
- Added support for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> integer `FOR` loops, which iterate over a range of integer values. [#130211](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130211)

### Operational changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">Admission Control</a> now has an integration for pacing snapshot ingest traffic based on disk bandwidth. `kvadmission.store.snapshot_ingest_bandwidth_control.enabled` is used to turn on this integration. It requires provisioned bandwidth to be set for the store (or cluster through the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> ) for it to take effect. [#131243](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131243)
- Added validation to check whether <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs" data-versioned="true">audit logging</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#log-buffering-for-network-sinks" data-versioned="true">buffering configurations</a> are both present in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#configure-log-sinks" data-versioned="true">file log sink</a>. Audit logging and buffering configuration should not both exist in the file log sink. [#132742](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132742)
- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#configure-log-sinks" data-versioned="true">file log sink</a> validation message. This would give clear indication to the user about the expected valid configuration. [#132899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132899)

### DB Console changes

- The value of the automatic <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> collection cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-automatic-collection-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.automatic_collection.enabled`</a> is now in the top right corner of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases**</a> overview page. [#132269](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132269)
- In the new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases**</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#tables-list-tab" data-versioned="true">**Tables**</a> pages, when cached data is being refreshed, the refresh button will be disabled and its tooltip text will display, `Data is currently refreshing`. [#132462](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132462)

### Bug fixes

- Addressed a rare bug that could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">backups</a> taken during a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-column" data-versioned="true">`DROP COLUMN`</a> operation with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">sequence</a> owner from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restoring</a> with the error: `rewriting descriptor ids: missing rewrite for <id> in SequenceOwner...`. [#132202](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132202)
- Fixed a bug existing since before v23.1 that could lead to incorrect results in rare cases. The bug requires a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">join</a> between two tables with an equality between columns with equivalent, but not identical <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/data-types" data-versioned="true">types</a> (e.g., `OID` and `REGCLASS` ). In addition, the join must lookup into an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> that includes a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a> that references one of the equivalent columns. [#126345](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126345)
- Fixed a bug existing since before v23.1 that could lead to incorrect results in rare cases. The bug requires a lookup <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">join</a> into a table with a computed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> column, where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a> expression is composite sensitive. A composite sensitive expression can compare differently if supplied non-identical but equivalent input values (e.g., `2.0::DECIMAL` versus `2.00::DECIMAL` ). [#126345](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126345)
- Fixed a bug that caused quotes around the name of a routine to be dropped when it was called within another <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">routine</a>. This could prevent the correct routine from being resolved if the nested routine name was case-sensitive. The bug has existed since v24.1 when nested routines were introduced. [#131643](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131643)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a> would print out the previous error message when executing the `quit` command. [#130736](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130736)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges#span-statistics" data-versioned="true">span statistics</a> request on a mixed-version cluster resulted in a null pointer exception. [#132349](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132349)
- Fixed an issue where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> would fail to update <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/protect-changefeed-data" data-versioned="true">protected timestamp records</a> in the face of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds#changefeed-retry-errors" data-versioned="true">retryable errors</a>. [#132712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132712)
- The [`franz-go`](https://github.com/twmb/franz-go) library has been updated to fix a potential deadlock on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> restarts. [#132761](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132761)
- Fixed a bug that in rare cases could cause incorrect evaluation of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions" data-versioned="true">scalar expressions</a> involving `NULL` values. [#132261](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132261)
- Fixed a bug in the query <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> that in rare cases could cause CockroachDB nodes to crash. The bug could occur when a query contains a filter in the form `col IN (elem0, elem1,..., elemN)` only when `N` is very large, (e.g., 1.6+ million), and when `col` exists in a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/hash-sharded-indexes" data-versioned="true">hash-sharded index</a>, or exists a table with an indexed, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a> dependent on `col`. [#132701](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132701)
- The `proretset` column of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog.pg_proc`</a> table is now properly set to `true` for set-returning built-in functions. [#132853](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132853)
- Fixed an error that could be caused by using an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`</a> expression that references a user-defined (or unknown) type name. These kinds of expressions are invalid, but previously the error was not handled properly. Now, a correct error message is returned. [#132348](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132348)

### Build changes

- Upgraded to Go v1.23.2. [#132111](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132111)

## v24.3.0-alpha.2

Release Date: October 14, 2024

### Downloads

<Warning>
CockroachDB v24.3.0-alpha.2 is a testing release. Testing releases are intended for testing and experimentation only, and are not qualified for production environments and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
</Warning>

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table><thead><tr><th>Operating System</th><th>Architecture</th><th>Full executable</th><th>SQL-only executable</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td rowspan="2">Linux</td><td>Intel</td><td><a
