### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-alpha.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-alpha.2 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-alpha.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-alpha.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.3.0-alpha.1...v24.3.0-alpha.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.3.0-alpha.1...v24.3.0-alpha.2)

### Security updates

- The parameters for an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authentication#hba-configuration-syntax" data-versioned="true">HBA config entry</a> for LDAP are now validated when the entry is created or amended, in addition to the validation that happens during an authentication attempt. [#132086](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132086)
- Added automatic cleanup and validation for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#default-privileges" data-versioned="true">default privileges</a> that reference dropped roles after a major-version upgrade to v24.3. [#131782](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131782)

### General changes

- Changed the license `cockroach` is distributed under to the new CockroachDB Software License (CSL). [#131799](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131799) [#131794](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131794) [#131793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131793)

### Enterprise edition changes

- You can now <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#authentication" data-versioned="true">authenticate to the DB console API</a> by supplying a Java Web Token (JWT) as a Bearer token in the Authorization header. [#130779](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130779)

### SQL language changes

- To view comments on a type, you can use the new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-types" data-versioned="true">`SHOW TYPES WITH COMMENT`</a> command. Comments can be added using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/comment-on" data-versioned="true">`COMMENT ON`</a>. [#131183](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131183)
- You can create or alter a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function (UDF)</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/stored-procedures" data-versioned="true">stored procedure (SP)</a> with `[EXTERNAL] SECURITY DEFINER` instead of the default `[EXTERNAL] SECURITY INVOKER`. With `SECURITY DEFINER`, the privileges of the owner are checked when the UDF or SP is executed, rather than the privileges of the executor. The `EXTERNAL` keyword is optional and exists for SQL language conformity. [#129720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129720)

### Operational changes

- The following new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> show details about <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replication</a> flow control send queue when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kvadmission.flow_control.enabled` is set to `true` and the cluster setting `kvadmission.flow_control.mode` is set to `apply_to_all`.
    - `kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.regular.deducted.prevent_send_queue`
    - `kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.elastic.deducted.prevent_send_queue`
    - `kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.elastic.deducted.force_flush_send_queue`
    - `kvflowcontrol.range_controller.count`
    - `kvflowcontrol.send_queue.bytes`
    - `kvflowcontrol.send_queue.count`
    - `kvflowcontrol.send_queue.prevent.count`
    - `kvflowcontrol.send_queue.scheduled.deducted_bytes`
    - `kvflowcontrol.send_queue.scheduled.force_flush`

        [#131857](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131857)
- The following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> have been renamed:

    <table><thead><tr><th>Previous name</th><th>New name-</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.disconnected</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.returned.disconnect</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.disconnected</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.returned.disconnect</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.regular.disconnected</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.regular.returned.disconnect</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.elastic.disconnected</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.send.elastic.returned.disconnect</code></td></tr></tbody></table>

    [#131857](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131857)

### Cluster virtualization changes

- The `_status/ranges/` endpoint on DB Console <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-debug-pages" data-versioned="true">Advanced debug pages</a> is now enabled for non-system virtual clusters, where it returns the ranges only for the tenant you are logged into. For the system virtual cluster, the `_status/ranges/` endpoint continues to return ranges for the specified node across all virtual clusters. [#131100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131100)

### DB Console changes

- Improved performance in the **Databases**, **Tables View**, and **Table Details** sections of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases page**</a> [#131769](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131769)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where JSON values returned by `cockroach` commands using the `--format=sql` flag were not correctly escaped if they contained double quotes within a string. [#131881](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131881)
- Fixed an error that could happen if an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#aggregate-functions" data-versioned="true">aggregate function</a> was used as the value in a `SET` command. [#131891](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131891)
- Fixed a rare bug introduced in v22.2 in which an update of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary key</a> column could fail to update the primary index if it is also the only column in a separate column family. [#131869](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131869)
- Fixed a rare bug where dropping a column of `FLOAT4`, `FLOAT8`, `DECIMAL`, `JSON`, `ARRAY`, or collate `STRING` type stored in a single <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column family</a> could prevent subsequent reading of the table if the column family was not the first column family. [#131967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131967)
- Fixed an `unimplemented` internal error that could occur when ordering by a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/vector" data-versioned="true">`VECTOR`</a> column. [#131703](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131703)

### Performance improvements

- Efficiency has been improved when writing string-like values over the PostgreSQL wire protocol. [#131964](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131964)
- Error handling during periodic table history polling has been improved when the `schema_locked` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/with-storage-parameter#table-parameters" data-versioned="true">table parameter</a> is not used. [#131951](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131951)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.3.0-alpha.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.3.0-alpha.1 on Github, visit [v24.3.0-alpha.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.3.0-alpha.1).

### Security updates

- URLs in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE CHANGEFEED`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE SCHEDULE FOR CHANGEFEED`</a> SQL statements are now sanitized of any secrets before being written to unredacted <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">logs</a>. [#126970](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126970)
- The LDAP <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `server.ldap_authentication.client.tls_certificate` and `server.ldap_authentication.client.tls_key` did not have callbacks installed to reload the settings value for LDAP authManager. This change fixes this by adding the necessary callbacks. [#131151](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131151)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">Cluster settings</a> for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authentication#authentication-configuration" data-versioned="true">host-based authentication</a> configuration ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-host-based-authentication-configuration" data-versioned="true">`server.host_based_authentication.configuration`</a> ) and identity map configuration ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`server.identity_map.configuration`</a> ) need to be redacted as they can be configured to contain LDAP bind usernames, passwords, and mapping of external identities to SQL users that are sensitive. These cluster settings can be configured for redaction via the `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` cluster setting. [#131150](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131150)
- Added support for configuring authorization using LDAP. During login, the list of groups that a user belongs to are fetched from the LDAP server. These groups are mapped to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-role" data-versioned="true">SQL roles</a> by extracting the common name (CN) from the group. After authenticating the user, the login flow grants these roles to the user, and revokes any other roles that are not returned by the LDAP server. The groups given by the LDAP server are treated as the sole source of truth for role memberships, so any roles that were manually granted to the user will not remain in place. [#131043](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131043)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authentication#authentication-configuration" data-versioned="true">host-based authentication</a> (HBA) configuration cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-host-based-authentication-configuration" data-versioned="true">`server.host_based_authentication.configuration`</a> was unable to handle double quotes in authentication method option values. For example, for the following entry:

    ```text
    host all all all ldap ldapserver=ldap.example.com ldapport=636 ldapbasedn="ou=users,dc=example,dc=com" ldapbinddn="cn=readonly,dc=example,dc=com" ldapbindpasswd=readonly_password ldapsearchattribute=uid ldapsearchfilter="(memberof=cn=cockroachdb_users,ou=groups,dc=example,dc=com)"
    ```

    The HBA parser would fail after incorrectly determining `ldapbinddn="cn=readonly,dc=example,dc=com"` as 2 separate options (`ldapbinddn=and cn=readonly,dc=example,dc=com`). Now, the 2 tokens are set as key and value respectively for the same HBA configuration option. [#131480](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131480)

### General changes

- CockroachDB will now avoid <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">logging</a> unnecessary stack traces while executing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">scheduled jobs</a>. [#129846](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129846)
- Upgrading to 24.3 is blocked if no <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs" data-versioned="true">license</a> is installed, or if a trial/free license is installed with telemetry disabled. [#130576](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130576)
- Attempting to install a second Enterprise trial license on the same cluster will now fail. [#131422](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131422)
- Changed the license `cockroach` is distributed under to the new CockroachDB Software License (CSL). [#131690](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131690) [#131686](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131686) [#131688](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131688) [#131687](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131687) [#131717](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131717) [#131689](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131689) [#131693](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131693) [#131691](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131691) [#131777](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131777) [#131778](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131778) [#131661](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131661)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a `CompressionLevel` field to the changefeed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka-sink-configuration" data-versioned="true">`kafka_sink_config`</a> option. <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">Changefeeds</a> will use this compression level when emitting events to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">Kafka sink</a>. The possible values depend on a compression codec. The `CompressionLevel` field optimizes for faster or stronger level of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka-sink-configuration" data-versioned="true">compression</a>. [#125456](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125456)
- The updated version of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">CockroachDB changefeed Kafka sink implementation</a> now supports specifying compression levels. [#127827](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127827)
- Introduced the cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`server.jwt_authentication.client.timeout`</a> to capture the HTTP client timeout for external calls made during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">JWT authentication</a>. [#127145](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127145)
- The JWT authentication <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> have been made `public`. [#128170](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128170)
- Updated certain error messages to refer to the `stable` docs tree rather than an explicit version. [#128842](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128842)
- Disambiguated <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/essential-metrics-self-hosted" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> and logs for the two buffers used by the KV feed. The affected metrics now have a suffix indicating which buffer they correspond to: `changefeed.buffer_entries.*`, `changefeed.buffer_entries_mem.*`, `changefeed.buffer_pushback_nanos.*`. The previous versions are still supported for backward compatibility, though using the new format is recommended. [#128813](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128813)
- Added support for authorization to a CockroachDB cluster via LDAP, retrieving AD groups membership information for LDAP user. The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authentication#authentication-configuration" data-versioned="true">HBA configuration</a> cluster setting option `ldapgrouplistfilter` performs filtered search query on LDAP for matching groups. An example HBA configuration entry to support LDAP authZ configuration:

    ```sql
    # TYPE    DATABASE      USER           ADDRESS             METHOD             OPTIONS
    # Allow all users to connect to using LDAP authentication with search and bind    host    all           all            all                 ldap               ldapserver=ldap.example.com ldapport=636 "ldapbasedn=ou=users,dc=example,dc=com" "ldapbinddn=cn=readonly,dc=example,dc=com" ldapbindpasswd=readonly_password ldapsearchattribute=uid "ldapsearchfilter=(memberof=cn=cockroachdb_users,ou=groups,dc=example,dc=com)" "ldapgrouplistfilter=(objectClass=groupOfNames)"
    # Fallback to password authentication for the root user
    host    all           root           0.0.0.0/0          password
    ```

    For example, to use for an Azure AD server:

    ```sql
    SET cluster setting server.host_based_authentication.configuration = 'host    all           all            all                 ldap ldapserver=azure.dev ldapport=636 "ldapbasedn=OU=AADDC Users,DC=azure,DC=dev" "ldapbinddn=CN=Some User,OU=AADDC Users,DC=azure,DC=dev" ldapbindpasswd=my_pwd ldapsearchattribute=sAMAccountName "ldapsearchfilter=(memberOf=CN=azure-dev-domain-sync-users,OU=AADDC Users,DC=crlcloud,DC=dev)" "ldapgrouplistfilter=(objectCategory=CN=Group,CN=Schema,CN=Configuration,DC=crlcloud,DC=dev)"
    host    all           root           0.0.0.0/0          password';
    ```

    Post configuration, the CockroachDB cluster should be able to authorize users via LDAP server if:

    1. Users LDAP authentication attempt is successful, and it has the user's DN for the LDAP server.
    2. `ldapgrouplistfilter` is properly configured, and it successfully syncs groups of the user. [#128498](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128498)
- Added changefeed support for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#mvcc-timestamp" data-versioned="true">`mvcc_timestamp`</a> option when the changefeed is emitting in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-messages#avro" data-versioned="true">`avro`</a> format. If both options are specified, the Avro schema includes an `mvcc_timestamp` metadata field and emits the row's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#mvcc" data-versioned="true">MVCC timestamp</a> with the row data. [#129840](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129840)
- Updated the cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-sink-io-workers" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.sink_io_workers`</a> with all the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">sinks</a> that support the setting. [#129946](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129946)
- Added a LDAP authentication method to complement password-based login for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> if HBA configuration has an entry for LDAP for the user attempting login, along with other matching criteria (like the requests originating IP address) for authentication to the DB Console. [#130418](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130418)
- Added timers around key parts of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> pipeline to help debug feeds experiencing issues. The `changefeed.stage.<stage>.latency` metrics now emit latency histograms for each stage. The metric respects the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds#using-changefeed-metrics-labels" data-versioned="true">changefeed `scope` label</a> for debugging specific feeds. [#128794](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128794)
- For <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/how-does-a-changefeed-work" data-versioned="true">enterprise changefeeds</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/eventlog" data-versioned="true">events</a> `changefeed_failed` and `create_changefeed` now include a `JobId` field. [#131396](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131396)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `seconds_until_license_expiry` allows you to monitor the status of a cluster's Enterprise license. [#129052](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129052).
- Added the `changefeed.total_ranges` metric, which <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">monitors</a> the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> that are watched by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/how-does-a-changefeed-work" data-versioned="true">changefeed aggregators</a>. It shares the same polling interval as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/advanced-changefeed-configuration#lagging-ranges" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.lagging_ranges`</a>, which is controlled by the existing `lagging_ranges_polling_interval` option. [#130897](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130897)

### SQL language changes

- Added a session setting, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">`optimizer_use_merged_partial_statistics`</a> which defaults to `false`. When set to `true`, it enables usage of existing partial <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> merged with full statistics when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizing</a> a query. [#126948](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126948)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">`enable_create_stats_using_extremes`</a> session setting is now `true` by default. Partial statistics at extremes can be collected using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-statistics" data-versioned="true">`CREATE STATISTICS <stat_name> ON <column_name> FROM <table_name> USING EXTREMES`</a> syntax. [#127850](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127850)
- Added <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schemas" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SCHEMAS WITH COMMENT`</a> and `SHOW SCHEMAS FROM database_name WITH COMMENT` functionality similar to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-tables" data-versioned="true">`SHOW TABLES`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-databases" data-versioned="true">`SHOW DATABASES`</a>. [#127816](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127816)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">`deadlock_timeout` session variable</a> is now supported. The configuration can be used to specify the time to wait on a lock before pushing the lock holder for deadlock detection. It can be set at session granularity. [#128506](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128506)
- Partial statistics at extremes can now be collected on all valid columns of a table using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-statistics" data-versioned="true">`CREATE STATISTICS <stat_name>` `FROM <table_name> USING EXTREMES`</a> syntax, without an `ON <col_name>` clause. Valid columns are all single column prefixes of a forward <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> excluding partial, sharded, and implicitly partitioned indexes. [#127836](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127836)
- Partial <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> can now be automatically collected at the extremes of indexes when a certain fraction and minimum number of rows are stale (by default 5% and 100 respectively). These can be configured with new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-and-reset-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">table storage parameters</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>, and the feature is disabled by default. The new cluster settings and table parameters are:
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.enabled` / `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_enabled`, defaults to `false`.
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.min_stale_rows` / `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_min_stale_rows`, defaults to `100`.
    - `sql.stats.automatic_partial_collection.fraction_stale_rows` / `sql_stats_automatic_partial_collection_fraction_stale_rows`, Defaults to `0.05`. [#93067](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93067)
- The session variable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#enforce-home-region-follower-reads-enabled" data-versioned="true">`enforce_home_region_follower_reads_enabled`</a> is now deprecated, and will be removed in a future release. The related session variable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#enforce-home-region" data-versioned="true">`enforce_home_region`</a> is **not** deprecated. [#129024](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129024)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to control whether most common values are collected as part of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#control-histogram-collection" data-versioned="true">histogram collection</a> for use by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a>. The setting is called `sql.stats.histogram_buckets.include_most_common_values.enabled`. When enabled, the histogram collection logic will ensure that the most common sampled values are represented as histogram bucket upper bounds. Since histograms in CockroachDB track the number of elements equal to the upper bound in addition to the number of elements less, this allows the optimizer to identify the most common values in the histogram and better estimate the rows processed by a query plan. To set the number of most common values to include in a histogram, a second setting `sql.stats.histogram_buckets.max_fraction_most_common_values` was added. Currently, the default is `0.1`, or `10%` of the number of buckets. With a 200 bucket histogram, by default, at most 20 buckets may be adjusted to include a most common value as the upper bound. [#129378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129378)
- Added a new column to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal#tables" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal.table_spans`</a> to indicate whether a table is <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-table" data-versioned="true">dropped</a>. Rows for dropped tables will be removed once they are <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collected</a>. [#128788](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128788)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.txn.repeatable_read_isolation.enabled`, which defaults to`false`. When set to `true`, the following statements will configure transactions to run under `REPEATABLE READ` isolation, rather than being automatically interpreted as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/demo-serializable" data-versioned="true">`SERIALIZABLE`</a>:
    - `BEGIN TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`
    - `SET TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`
    - `SET default_transaction_isolation = 'repeatable read'`
    - `SET SESSION CHARACTERISTICS AS TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL REPEATABLE READ`

        This setting was added since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#comparison-to-ansi-sql-isolation-levels" data-versioned="true">`REPEATABLE READ` transactions</a> is a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachdb-feature-availability" data-versioned="true">preview</a> feature, so usage of it is opt-in for v24.3. In a future CockroachDB major version, this setting will change to default to `true`. [#130089](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130089)
- Previously, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`</a> showed the changefeed jobs for the last 14 days by default. Now, it uses the same age filter for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW JOBS`</a>, which shows jobs from the last 12 hours by default. [#127584](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127584)
- Set the default for session variable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#large-full-scan-rows" data-versioned="true">`large_full_scan_rows`</a> to `0`. This means that by default, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#disallow-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">`disallow_full_table_scans`</a> will disallow **all** <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">full table scans</a>, even full scans on very small tables. If `large_full_scan_rows` is set &gt; 0, `disallow_full_table_scans` will allow full scans estimated to read fewer than `large_full_scan_rows`. [#131040](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131040)
- It is now possible to create <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> trigger functions, which can be executed by a trigger in response to table mutation events. Note that this patch does not add support for triggers, only trigger functions. [#126734](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126734)
- Cluster settings <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-enterprise-license" data-versioned="true">`enterprise.license`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-diagnostics-reporting-enabled" data-versioned="true">`diagnostics.reporting.enabled`</a> now have additional validation. [#131097](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131097)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SESSIONS`</a> command was changed to include an `authentication_method` column in the result. This column will show the method used to authenticate the session, for example, `password`, `cert`, `LDAP`, etc. [#131625](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131625)

### Operational changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/eventlog" data-versioned="true">Events</a> `DiskSlownessDetected` and `DiskSlownessCleared` are now logged when disk slowness is detected and cleared on a store. [#127025](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127025)
- Several <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> allow you to configure rate-limiting traffic to cloud storage over various protocols. These settings begin with `cloudstorage`. [#127207](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127207)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.range.range_size_hard_cap` allows you to limit how large a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">range</a> can grow before <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#split-failed-while-applying-backpressure-are-rows-updated-in-a-tight-loop" data-versioned="true">backpressure</a> is applied. This can help to mitigate against a situation where a range cannot be split, such as when a range is comprised of a single key due to an issue with the schema or workload pattern or a bug in client application code. The default is 8 GiB, which is 16 times the default max range size. If you have changed the max range size, you may need to adjust this cluster setting or reduce the range size. [#129450](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129450)
- The following `kvflowcontrol` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> have been renamed. After a cluster is finalized on v24.3, old and new metrics will be populated. The previous metrics under `kvasdmission.flow_controller` will be removed.

    <table><thead><tr><th>Old metric names</th><th>New metric names</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;tokens&#95;available</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.available</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;tokens&#95;available</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.available</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;tokens&#95;deducted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.deducted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;tokens&#95;deducted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.deducted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;tokens&#95;returned</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.returned</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;tokens&#95;returned</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.returned</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;tokens&#95;unaccounted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.regular.unaccounted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;tokens&#95;unaccounted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.tokens.eval.elastic.unaccounted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;stream&#95;count</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.streams.eval.regular.total&#95;count</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;stream&#95;count</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.streams.eval.elastic.total&#95;count</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;requests&#95;waiting</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.regular.requests.waiting</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;requests&#95;waiting</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.elastic.requests.waiting</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;requests&#95;admitted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.regular.requests.admitted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;requests&#95;admitted</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.elastic.requests.admitted</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;requests&#95;errored</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.regular.requests.errored</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;requests&#95;errored</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.elastic.requests.errored</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;requests&#95;bypassed</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.regular.requests.bypassed</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;requests&#95;bypassed</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.elastic.requests.bypassed</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.regular&#95;wait&#95;duration</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.regular.duration</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>kvadmission.flow&#95;controller.elastic&#95;wait&#95;duration</code></td><td><code>kvflowcontrol.eval&#95;wait.elastic.duration</code></td></tr></tbody></table>

    [#130167](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130167)
- The new `ranges.decommissioning` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> shows the number of ranges with a replica on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown" data-versioned="true">decommissioning</a> node. [#130117](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130117)
- New <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> have been added which control the refresh behavior for the cached data in the **Databases** page of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>:
    - `obs.tablemetadatacache.data_valid_duration`: the duration for which the data in `system.table_metadata` is considered valid before a cache reset will occur. Default: 20 minutes.
    - `obs.tablemetadatacache.automatic_updates.enabled`: whether to automatically update the cache according the validity interval. Default: `false`.

        [#130198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130198)
- New gauge <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> `security.certificate.expiration.{cert-type}` and `security.certificate.ttl.{cert-type}` show the expiration and TTL for a certificate. [#130110](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130110)
- To set the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/log-formats" data-versioned="true">logging format</a> for `stderr`, you can now set the `format` field to any valid format, rather than only `crdb-v2-tty`. [#131529](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131529)
- The following new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> show connection latency for each SQL authentication method:

    <table><thead><tr><th>Authentication method</th><th>Metric</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Certificate</td><td><code>auth&#95;cert&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr><tr><td>Java Web Token (JWT)</td><td><code>auth&#95;jwt&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr><tr><td>Kerberos GSS</td><td><code>auth&#95;gss&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr><tr><td>LDAP</td><td><code>auth&#95;ldap&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr><tr><td>Password</td><td><code>auth&#95;password&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr><tr><td>SCRAM SHA-256</td><td><code>auth&#95;scram&#95;conn&#95;latency</code></td></tr></tbody></table>

    [#131578](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131578)
- Verbose logging of slow <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#pebble" data-versioned="true">Pebble</a> reads can no longer be enabled via the shorthand flag `--vmodule=pebble_logger_and_tracer=2`, where `pebble_logger_and_tracer` contains the CockroachDB implementation of the logger needed by Pebble. Instead, you must list the Pebble files that contain the log statements. For example `--vmodule=reader=2,table=2`. [#127066](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127066)
- The lowest <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> priority for the storage layer has been renamed from `ttl-low-pri` to `bulk-low-pri`. [#129564](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129564)
- New clusters will now have a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-zone-configurations" data-versioned="true">zone configuration</a> defined for the `timeseries` range, which specifies `gc.ttlseconds` and inherits all other attributes from the zone config of the `default` range. This zone config will also be added to a cluster that is <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgraded</a> to v24.3 if it does not already have a zone config defined.[#128032](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128032)

### Command-line changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-tsdump" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug tsdump`</a> now includes all the available resolutions in the time range supplied by the user. [#127186](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127186)
- Added the flag `--tenant-name-scope` to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-cert#create-the-certificate-and-key-pair-for-a-client" data-versioned="true">`cert create-client`</a> command. This allows users to generate tenant-scoped <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/authentication#client-authentication" data-versioned="true">client certificates</a> using tenant names in addition to tenant IDs. [#129216](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129216)

### DB Console changes

- If a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">range</a> is larger than twice the max range size, it will now display in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-debug-pages" data-versioned="true">**Problem Ranges** page</a> in the DB Console. [#129001](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129001)
- Updated some metric charts on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Overview</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Replication</a> dashboards to omit verbose details in the legends for easier browsing. [#129149](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129149)
- Updated the icon for notification alerts to use the new CockroachDB logo. [#130333](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130333)
- The `txn.restarts.writetoooldmulti` metric was rolled into the `txn.restarts.writetooold` metric in the v24.1.0-alpha.1 release. `txn.restarts.writetoooldmulti` has now been removed altogether. [#131642](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131642)
- The grants table in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#databases" data-versioned="true">DB Details</a> page will now show the database level grants. For example, when clicking a database in the databases list. Previously, it showed grants per table in the database. [#131250](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131250)
- Added new database pages that are available from the side navigation **Databases** link. [#131594](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131594)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> will reflect any throttling behavior from the cluster due to an expired license or missing telemetry data. Enterprise licenses are not affected. [#131326](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131326)
- Users can hover over the node/region cell in multi-region deployments to view a list of nodes the database or table is on. [#130704](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130704)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** pages</a> in the DB console have been updated to read cached metadata about database and table storage statistics. The cache update time is now displayed in the top right-hand corner of the database and tables list pages. Users may trigger a cache refresh with the **refresh** icon next to the last updated time. The cache will also update automatically when users visit a **Databases** page and the cache is older than or equal to 20 minutes. [#131463](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131463)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate an `IS NOT NULL` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause#filter-rows" data-versioned="true">filter</a> if it was applied to non- `NULL` tuples that had `NULL` elements (like `(1, NULL)` or `(NULL, NULL)` ). The bug was present since v20.2. [#126901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126901)
- Fixed a bug related to displaying the names of composite types in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLES`</a> command. The names are now shown as two-part names, which disambiguates the output and makes it more portable to other databases. [#127158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127158)
- The `CONCAT()` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a> now accepts arguments of any data type. [#127098](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127098)
- Fixed a bug that prevented merged <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> from being created after injecting statistics or recreating <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">statement bundles</a>. This would occur when the injected statistics or statement bundle contained related full and partial statistics. [#127252](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127252)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could encounter spurious `(error encountered after some results were delivered)` `ERROR: context canceled` errors in rare cases when evaluating some queries. The bug was present since v22.2. The conditions that triggered the bug were queries that:
    - Had to be executed locally.
    - Had a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/limit-offset" data-versioned="true">`LIMIT`</a>.
    - Have at least two <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries#union-combine-two-queries" data-versioned="true">`UNION`</a> clauses.
    - Have some lookup or index <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> in the `UNION` branches. [#127076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127076)
- Updated the restore <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> description from `RESTORE... FROM` to `RESTORE FROM {backup} IN {collectionURI}` to reflect the new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> syntax. [#127970](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127970)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a `CASE` statement with multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries" data-versioned="true">subqueries</a> to produces the side effects of one of the subqueries even if that subquery shouldn't have been evaluated. [#120327](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120327)
- Changed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changer</a> ’s merge process so that it can detect <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transaction-retry-error-reference" data-versioned="true">contention errors</a> and automatically retry with a smaller batch size. This makes the merge process more likely to succeed without needing to manually tune settings. [#128201](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128201)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE ALL TYPES`</a> now shows corresponding type comments in its output. [#128084](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128084)
- Enforce the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">`statement_timeout` session setting</a> when waiting for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs</a> after a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> in an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#individual-statements" data-versioned="true">implicit transaction</a>. [#128474](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128474)
- Fixed a bug where certain dropdowns in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> appeared to be empty (with no options to select from) for users of the Safari browser. [#128996](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128996)
- Fixed a bug that would cause the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">`hlc_to_timestamp` function</a> to return an incorrect <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/timestamp" data-versioned="true">timestamp</a> for some input <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">decimals</a>. [#129153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129153)
- Fixed a memory leak where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">statement insight</a> objects could leak if the session was closed without the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transaction</a> finishing. [#128400](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128400)
- Fixed a bug in the public preview <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#write-ahead-log-wal-failover" data-versioned="true">WAL failover</a> feature that could prevent a node from starting if it crashed during a failover. [#129331](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129331)
- Fixed a bug where `'infinity'::TIMESTAMP` returned a different result than PostgreSQL. [#127141](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127141)
- Fixed a spurious error log from the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-queues-dashboard#replication-queue" data-versioned="true">replication queue</a> involving the text `" needs lease, not adding"`. [#129351](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129351)
- Using more than one <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql#structure" data-versioned="true">`DECLARE`</a> statement in the definition of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a> now correctly declares additional variables. [#129951](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129951)
- Fixed a bug in which some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR SHARE`</a> queries using `NOWAIT` could still block on locked rows when using the `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/demo-serializable" data-versioned="true">serializable</a> isolation. This bug was introduced with `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` in v23.2.0. [#130103](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130103)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrade</a> pre-condition for repairing descriptor corruption that could lead to finalization being stuck. [#130064](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130064)
- Fixed a bug that caused the optimizer to plan unnecessary post-query uniqueness checks during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> statements on tables with partial, unique, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/hash-sharded-indexes" data-versioned="true">hash-sharded indexes</a>. These unnecessary checks added overhead to execution of these statements, and caused the statements to error when executed under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED` isolation</a>. [#130366](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130366)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect evaluation of `CASE`, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#conditional-and-function-like-operators" data-versioned="true">`COALESCE`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#conditional-and-function-like-operators" data-versioned="true">`IF`</a> expressions with branches producing fixed-width string-like types, such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`CHAR`</a>. In addition, the `BPCHAR` type no longer incorrectly imposes a length limit of `1`. [#129007](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129007)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones" data-versioned="true">zone configuration</a> changes issued by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> were not blocked if a table had the `schema_locked` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/with-storage-parameter" data-versioned="true">storage parameter</a> set. [#130670](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130670)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples" data-versioned="true">`CHANGEFEED`</a> from being able to resume after being paused for a prolonged period of time. [#130622](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130622)
- Fixed a bug where if a client connection was attempting a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> while the same <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/schema-design-overview" data-versioned="true">schema objects</a> were being dropped, it was possible for the connection to be incorrectly dropped. [#130928](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130928)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that could cause incorrect results when:
    1. The query contained a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries#correlated-subqueries" data-versioned="true">correlated subquery</a>.
    2. The correlated subquery had a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause#group-by-an-alias" data-versioned="true">`GROUP BY`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#avoid-select-distinct-for-large-tables" data-versioned="true">`DISTINCT`</a> operator with an outer-column reference in its input.
    3. The correlated subquery was in the input of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause" data-versioned="true">`SELECT`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">`JOIN`</a> operator.
    4. The `SELECT` or `JOIN` had a filter that set the outer-column reference from (2) equal to a non-outer column in the input of the grouping operator.
    5. The grouping column set did not include the replacement column, and functionally determined the replacement column. [#130925](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130925)
- Fixed a bug which could cause errors with the message `"internal error: Non-nullable column..."` when executing statements under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED`</a> isolation that involved tables with `NOT NULL` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns#create-a-virtual-computed-column-using-jsonb-data" data-versioned="true">virtual columns</a>. [#130725](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130725)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a very rare internal error `"lists in SetPrivate are not all the same length"` when executing queries. [#130981](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130981)
- Fixed a bug that could cause incorrect evaluation of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions" data-versioned="true">scalar expressions</a> involving `NULL` values in rare cases. [#128123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128123)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE ALL SCHEMAS`</a> now shows corresponding schema comments in its output. [#130164](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130164)
- Fixed a bug, introduced in v23.2.0, where creating a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-full-and-incremental-backups#incremental-backups" data-versioned="true">incremental schedule</a> (using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-backup-schedule" data-versioned="true">`ALTER BACKUP SCHEDULE`</a> ) on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-full-and-incremental-backups#full-backups" data-versioned="true">full backup schedule</a> created on an older version would fail. [#131231](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131231)
- Fixed a bug that could cause an internal error if a table with an implicit ( `rowid` ) <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary key</a> was locked from within a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries" data-versioned="true">subquery</a> like `SELECT * FROM (SELECT * FROM foo WHERE x = 2) FOR UPDATE;`. The error could occur either under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED`</a> isolation, or with the `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> enabled. [#129768](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129768)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs</a> created in a session with non-zero session <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#set-time-zone" data-versioned="true">timezone offsets</a> could hang before starting, or report incorrect creation times when viewed in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW JOBS`</a> and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#123632](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123632)
- Fixed a bug which could result in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-changefeed#create-a-scheduled-changefeed-with-cdc-queries" data-versioned="true">changefeeds using CDC queries</a> failing due to a system table being <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collected</a>. [#131027](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131027)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#convert-to-a-different-data-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER COLUMN TYPE`</a> now errors out when there is a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial index</a> that is dependent on the column being altered. [#131590](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131590)
- Fixed a bug that prevented buffered file sinks from being included when iterating over all file sinks. This led to problems such as the `debug zip` command not being able to fetch logs for a cluster where buffering was enabled. [#130158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130158)
- Fixed a bug where backup schedules could advance a protected timestamp too early, which caused incremental backups to fail. [#131358](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131358)

### Performance improvements

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft-logs" data-versioned="true">Raft log</a> sync callback handling is now parallelized, which can improve write-heavy workload performance on large, single-store nodes. [#126523](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126523)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">Planning time</a> for complex queries has been reduced. [#128049](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128049)
- Reduced the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#write-amplification" data-versioned="true">write-amplification</a> impact of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">rebalances</a> by splitting snapshot SSTable files into smaller ones before ingesting them into <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#pebble" data-versioned="true">Pebble</a>. [#127997](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127997)
- Improved the performance of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job-system</a> related queries. [#123848](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123848)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query optimizer</a> now plans limited, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial-index scans</a> in more cases. [#129901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129901)
- The initialization of the execution engine for a query is now more efficient when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plan</a> contains <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#aggregate-functions" data-versioned="true">aggregate functions</a>. [#130834](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130834)
- Enabled multi-level <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#compaction" data-versioned="true">compactions</a> that moderately reduce <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#write-amplification" data-versioned="true">write amplification</a> within the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer" data-versioned="true">storage engine</a>. [#131378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131378)
- Increased the per-vCPU concurrency limits for KV operations. Specifically, increased the `kv.dist_sender.concurrency_limit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to 384/vCPU (up from 64/vCPU) and `kv.streamer.concurrency_limit` to 96/vCPU (up from 8/vCPU). [#131226](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131226)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now plans more efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup joins</a> in some cases. [#131383](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131383)

### Build changes

- Changed the AWS SDK version used for interactions with external storage from v1 to v2. [#129938](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129938)
